## D95 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-1**: officer derivation into the existing command + field pipes (the persona becomes the source of truth) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first wiring increment of the D94 rating system (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§9 R-1). The documented persona now SEEDS the levers the two pipes already read вҖ” **strategic** `gen.skill` and **tactical** officer `quality`/`radius`/`fate` вҖ” with the no-fudge keystone intact (the persona only sets inputs at build/make time; nothing is read at casualty/winner/rout time) and every unrated/un-opted entity **byte-identical**.
- **Strategic leg (`src/35-command.js`):** new `_cmdGenPersona(gen)` + `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen)`; `_cmdGenRating` now derives `skill` from the linked persona (`command/tactical/discipline` вҶ’ `fldOfficerSkillSeed`) instead of reading the static `gen.skill`. **Calibration oracle (strategic):** the 9 personas are authored so `round(0.45*command+0.35*tactical+0.20*discipline) === the Verified gen.skill EXACTLY` (FP-boundary-safe; min distance from the round-half boundary 0.2) вҶ’ `commandLeadership`/auto-resolve/conditioning stay **byte-identical** and the appoint-pool words still match history, while the persona is now the source. `cmdActiveTraits.skill` + the Command-desk Skill bar also route through `_cmdEffectiveSkill` (one source of truth; the bug-hunt critic's single-source-of-truth fix вҖ” byte-identical today, closes the future-drift footgun). Unrated generals keep authored `gen.skill`.
- **Tactical leg (`src/tactical/T3-officers.js`):** new `fldOfficerPersona(o)` + `fldMakeOfficer` derives `quality` (`fldPersonaQuality`, calibrated to reproduce the authored field quality within вүӨ0.005 вҖ” the R-0 oracle, so a rated aura shifts only slightly), `radius` (authored echelon range + a small charisma nudge, clamped 160вҖ“290), and `fate` (the persona's durability multiplier, which matches the authored scenario fate for the Bull Run cast). **EXPLICIT `pid` opt-in, NO `id` fallback** вҖ” the bug-hunt-class fix for a real **cross-scenario id collision**: leader ids are reused across battles (`ld_jackson` is the 1861 brigadier at Bull Run but a corps commander at Antietam/Chancellorsville), so an `id`-match would leak the wrong persona; a leader derives ONLY when it names a persona via `pid`. The 7 Bull Run leaders are opted in (`data/bullrun.json`); every other scenario's leaders have no `pid` вҶ’ byte-identical until their personas are authored.
- **`data/ratings.json` вҖ” NEW `generalPersonas` map** (9 strategic army-commander personas keyed by the `data/generals.json` id): **CS** Lee, Jackson, A.S. Johnston, Bragg, Longstreet В· **US** McClellan, Grant, Burnside, Meade вҖ” the principal commanders of the 9 D92-hardened battles (Bull Run is covered by the field cast). A SEPARATE record from the Bull Run FIELD cast (war-long army commander vs the 1861 brigade officer); R-5 unifies them into one prosopography person. The documented character + the named negatives (McClellan `the_slows`, Burnside `rigid_plan`, Bragg `piecemeal`) are Verified with real sources (Sears 1988, Marvel 1991, Robertson 1997, Hess 2016, Wert 1993, Chernow 2017, McPherson 1988, вҖҰ); the attribute VECTOR is Inferred designer calibration anchored to each Verified `gen.skill`; `aggression` tracks the documented temperament and is EXCLUDED from the headline OVR (anti-Lost-Cause).
- **Vetting:** GATE OK; `probe-ratings` **13/13** (3 new R-1 steps: strategic exact + unrated byte-identical + tactical derive + cross-scenario collision guard), `probe-command` **15/15** (incl. the new source-of-truth guard); FULL no-regression GREEN вҖ” all 9 battle baselines byte-identical (incl. **chancellorsville 24/24**, proving the `ld_jackson` collision fix) + roster/custom-builder/fog/ai/autopause/campaign-link/logistics/arms/presets/csplayer/officers/field/engineering-corps/tactical-visuals; diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors. **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 Opus lenses Г— default-refute verify + a completeness critic): 0 confirmed finder findings; 1 LOW critic finding (the single-source-of-truth read) FIXED. ## D96 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-2**: the OVR read-out UI (Command desk grades + tactical HUD brigade OVR) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)

## D97 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-3**: the badge engine (the first ratingвҶ’combat seam) + the no-fudge build-gate вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first place a rating actually TOUCHES combat (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§4/В§6/В§9 R-3). A guarded one-token factor seeds the levers the engine already reads; the no-fudge OUTPUT wall is now enforced **structurally** by the build. **Byte-identical when off** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles produce identical deterministic results on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build).
- **`fldBadgeFactor(u, lever)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** the guarded MULTIPLICATIVE one-token factor вҖ” IDENTITY 1.0 when `__FIELD.badges` is off OR the unit carries no matching badge (mirrors the `(u.cmdBonus||0)` no-op). It sums the unit's badges' signed `mag`s for a lever, gates each by its trigger (`_fldBadgeTrig`: always/march/in_woods/arm_cav/arm_art; others default on, an R-4 refinement), then CLAMPS the summed delta to the realism-scaled per-unit per-lever cap (`fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"badgeLever")` вҖ” arcade .16 / balanced .10 / historian .06, D94-softcap). Negatives are DAMPERS (factor<1, вүҘ1вҲ’cap), never enemy buffs. Pure read; returns a factor, never writes state. Plus `fldUnitCohesion(u)` ((cohesionвҲ’50)/50, clamped [вҲ’1,1]; **0 when cohesion unauthored** вҶ’ byte-identical вҖ” the rally term defaults neutral, NOT xp-derived, since an xp-derived default would shift the rally of every xpвү 2 unit).
- **Four guarded seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** fire (`fldResolveFire` `power *= fldBadgeFactor(u,"fire")`), rally (`fldMoraleStep` `rally = (1 + xp*.12*vet + .06*cohesion*vet) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"rally")`), melee (`fldResolveMelee` atk/def), speed (`fldMoveFactor` `(u._spdMul||1) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"speed")` вҖ” `_spdMul` reserved for the R-4 X-Factor surge). All identity when off. The `__FIELD.badges` gate (default ON, `_badgesOff` hook) + `__FIELD.realismTier` (set in `fldPresetsApply`, default balanced) added.
- **Badge data (`data/ratings.json`):** each of the 25 badgeDefs now carries `fldLever` (fire/rally/speed/melee, or `none` for officer-aura / auto-resolve-edge / canister / sight effects deferred to R-4/В§7.5) + a signed `mag`. Ships the Star/Superstar positives + the Verified named negatives with real tactical bite: McClellan **The Slows** (speed вҲ’0.08), Bragg **Piecemeal** (rally вҲ’0.05), Burnside **Rigid Plan** (fire вҲ’0.05), **Green Levies** (rally вҲ’0.08), **Powder-Shy** (rally вҲ’0.05); positives marksman/woods_fighter (fire), disciplined/blooded/beloved/stonewall (rally), hardy_marcher/horseman (speed). Badges are NOT yet assigned to shipped scenario rosters (that is the R-6 sweep) вҶ’ every battle stays byte-identical.
- **The NO-FUDGE OUTPUT WALL, build-gate-asserted (`tools/build.mjs` gate 4d):** the rating module (`tactical/T14-ratings.js`) is scanned at build for any write to `cas`/`aCas`/`bCas`/`.victory`/`.men`/`sev.*` вҖ” dot AND bracket notation (the bracket variants close the bug-hunt's computed-member bypass) вҖ” and the build FAILS (exit 5) if found. Verified firing on planted `u.men=0`, `u["men"]=0`, and `F.sev["attrition"]=2` writes; clean build prints `GATE OK В· вҖҰ В· no-fudge вң“`. The combat modules legitimately write these; the wall scopes to the rating/badge module, which may only seed inputs + return factors.
- **Vetting вҖ” NOTE the environmental deviation:** GATE OK (incl. the new no-fudge gate). The standard `load`-based probe suite was **environmentally BLOCKED** this session: headless Chrome's `load` event never fires for the game page (the THREE-CDN `<script>` stalls in headless intermittently; it broke the committed-green R-2 build identically; a trivial page fires `load` in 73ms; `domcontentloaded` loads everything incl. THREE in ~1.5s). Root contributors: (a) the single-threaded `python -m http.server` chokes on the page's ~170 local asset requests (fixed by a **ThreadingHTTPServer**); (b) the THREE-CDN `load` stall (the documented gotcha). So R-3 was vetted via a **`domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness** (`.tmp/r3-verify.mjs`): it ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically (same seed) on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build and confirmed **IDENTICAL** casualties/winner/steps for all 10, plus the full badge-logic assertions (off=1, single=1.06, stack clamps to 1.10=1+cap, realism arc 1.16 > bal 1.10 > his 1.06, negatives 0.92, cohesion math), 0 pageerrors. This cross-build diff is a *stronger* byte-identity check than the standard probes. **Adversarial bug-hunt** (4 Opus lenses Г— refute-verify + critic): 2 confirmed (the gate-4d bracket bypass вҖ” FIXED by adding bracket regexes; a phantom `'sharpshooters'` key in the probe/T0 comment вҖ” FIXED) + 0 critic. Committed + pushed.

## D98 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-4**: the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" Madden surge, inside the no-fudge wall) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The dramatic increment (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§4/В§6/В§9 R-4, D94 fork-1 "DRAMATIC surge"). An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and SURGES on ONE channel, hard-capped вҖ” a visible, announced swing that provably can never breach the no-fudge wall. **Byte-identical when off / unassigned** (proven: a `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically on the R-4 build vs the committed R-3 build (HEAD dc9ba61) вҶ’ **IDENTICAL** winner/US-cas/CS-cas/steps for all 10, 0 pageerrors).
- **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), tests its activation (`_fldXFactorInZone`: march_vigor=moving В· his_offensive=moving/charging В· ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging В· last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) В· usct_assault/mass_assault=charging В· flanking=cav & charging) and, when in the zone, sets the surge on EXACTLY ONE channel (its declared lever): a **NON-speed** X-Factor (rally/melee/none) sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a **SPEED** X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT surge the command aura. One-shot вҡЎ `fldAnnounce` + `fldScenarioBanner` on the rising edge (`_xfOn`); a marker glow (`_xfGlow`); deterministic decay (`_fldXfDecay`) toward identity out of zone. **NO RNG** вҶ’ seed-replayable. A unit carrying no X-Factor is left wholly untouched (`_xf*`/`_spdMul` stay undefined) вҶ’ byte-identical.
- **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** scales the unit's ALREADY-SUMMED command aura `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` вҖ” pushes the aura toward the **hard 0.9 wall, NEVER beyond**. A strict no-op unless an X-Factor is active (`_xfActive` undefined/вүӨ1) вҶ’ byte-identical. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (so the aura is summed first), gated on `__FIELD.badges` (NOT officers) so the cmdBonus surge and the `_spdMul` surge share ONE gate.
- **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` calls `fldXFactorStep(dt)` just before `fldOfficersStep` + the apply loop just after; `fldMoveFactor` clamps the **COMBINED** speed factor (the `_spdMul` surge Г— the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** so no stack can breach it (exactly 1 when no rating speed input вҶ’ byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` pulse вҖ” a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries the meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font/tofu dependency), `reduceMotion`-honored, drawn for no shipped unit вҶ’ byte-identical.
- **Data (`data/ratings.json`):** ADDED `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav, flanking trigger, fldLever none вҶ’ surges via the capped cmdBonus only; 2 sources вҶ’ Verified). The 7 X-Factors: foot_cavalry, rock_of_chickamauga, bayonet, earned_in_blood, grand_charge, first_with_the_most, the_slows. NOT assigned to any shipped scenario (the R-6 sweep) вҶ’ byte-identical.
- **NO-FUDGE REPLAY GATE (`tools/probe-ratings.mjs`, +2 steps вҶ’ 17/17):** a deterministic seed-replay tags one CS sandbox brigade with foot_cavalry and runs it vs the untagged baseline (same seed): the surge **BITES** (it flipped a US win into a CS win) yet stays **bounded** (17.2% total-casualty delta вҖ” an input nudge, not a scripted result) and the **wall holds** (`maxCmd 0.47 < 0.9`). Plus synthetic asserts: speed X-Factor surges only `_spdMul` (no cmdBonus), non-speed surges cmdBonus capped at the wall, the combined-speed clamp binds at 1.30, negatives drag, realism-monotone amp, decayвҶ’1.

## D100 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q8**: the between-battle CAMP LOOP (drilling + progression) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The agency that GROWS your rating over a campaign (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§15 / В§14.6). A new "Camp" desk tab where, between battles, the President DRILLS the army; the drilled training raises the army he fields via a guarded, bounded conditioning seam вҖ” PURE INPUT-SEEDING, never the scoreboard, and **byte-identical until the player engages the camp**.
- **`src/36-camp.js` (new module):** `campInit` (idempotent; seeds `C.president.camp` = drill{musketry/maneuver/entrenching/endurance}, fatigue, delegate, **engaged**); `campDrill(C,focus)` (raises a focus toward CEIL 90, +fatigue, sets engaged); `campSetDelegate`; `campTrainingBonus(C)` (THE BRIDGE SEAM вҖ” per-facet deltas, ALL ZERO when no focus is drilled); `campOnResolve` (rest sheds fatigue, a delegated army auto-drills, a clean win SEASONS / a battle this side bled the lion's share ERODES вҖ” gated on `engaged`); `campRenderTab`/`campWireTab`; `_campGrade`/`_campBar`. **Drilling/progression only** вҖ” SCOUTING deferred to Q8b (it needs the strategic-next-battle вҶ” tactical-OOB mapping).
- **The bridge seam (`src/85-battle-bridge.js`):** `bridgeArmy` applies a guarded camp term вҖ” drilling lifts firepower (musketry) / morale (maneuver) / supply (entrenching) + relieves fatigue (endurance) + a small overall "sharpness," **bounded** (full-drill вүҲ +8 overall over base, вүӨ14; fatigue DRAGS the gain Г—(1вҲ’0.6В·fat/100)). EXACTLY 0 when undrilled вҶ’ byte-identical. Computed once, reused.
- **Wiring:** `campInit` in `_t1InitAll` (after cmdInit); `campOnResolve` in `_t1Resolve` (after cmdOnResolve); a "Camp" tab in `30-president-shell.js` (dispatch + tab arrays + button + wiring); `"36-camp.js"` in the manifest. `C.president.camp` rides `serializeSave` wholesale + lazy-migrates via idempotent campInit вҖ” **no `_SAVE_VER` bump** (additive, D7).
- **THE KEYSTONE (byte-identity):** an `engaged` flag (false until the first drill/delegate) makes the WHOLE loop INERT until the player opens the camp вҖ” `campOnResolve` early-returns and `campTrainingBonus` is all-zero at zero drill вҖ” so a campaign that never camps conditions byte-for-byte as the pre-Q8 build (proven: probe-camp's keystone step + probe-bridge 6/6 + probe-conditioning 6/6 UNCHANGED). NO RNG (deterministic).

ALL fixed: **(MED + a critic-MED, the real one)** the "bloody" attrition test divided a raw men-count by `C.manpower.strength` вҖ” a 0-100 INDEX (and one decremented upstream the same turn by manpowerOnResolve), so nearly every real battle read "bloody" вҶ’ the **win-seasons branch was effectively DEAD** (drilled training only ever decayed, inverting the headline progression). ## D101 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-5**: the PROSOPOGRAPHY SCALE-OUT (bulk per-person derivation + LAZY materialization + the play-as-anyone hook) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The D93 "Soldier's Story" substrate the whole rating spine was built for: a brigade can now be *inspected down to its men*, and any person can be *materialized + promoted* вҖ” all PURE DATA + DISPLAY, **byte-identical** (no shipped scenario assigns bulk persons; the deterministic sim вҖ” sandbox + all 9 battles вҖ” is proven identical to committed HEAD `84c5e95`). Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§5/В§8/В§9 R-5/В§15 (R9).
- **The LAZY-MATERIALIZATION keystone (В§8):** a brigade TOKEN carries ONE aggregate `fldMenMeanOVR(u,year)` вҖ” its men's mean OVR, derived O(1) from xp + arm-branch + year + a deterministic per-brigade-id jitter, clamped [20,88] (a brigade AVERAGE never reaches the Legendary individual ceiling). Per-person rows are NEVER instantiated en masse: `fldMaterializePerson(spec,year)` builds exactly ONE row on demand (inspect / play-as), and `fldBrigadeMuster(u,n,year)` builds a HARD-CAPPED (вүӨ6) representative sample (captain/sergeant/private from a data-driven `musterTemplate`), **never `u.men` rows** вҖ” proven: a 100,000-man brigade still materializes 3. The mean is always recomputable, never the source of truth.
- **New pure functions (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** `fldMenMeanOVR` В· `fldMaterializePerson` (reuses the R-0 `fldDerivePerson` вҶ’ headline + dual OVR + grade; a generated row gets a deterministic synthesized period name [`_fldSynthName` + `_FLD_FIRST`/`_FLD_LAST`, NO RNG] + Inferred provenance + a `latentCommand` seed) В· `fldPromotePerson(person,toRank)` (the **latent-command promotion** = play-as-anyone: lifts command/tactical/discipline/charisma by the rank-base delta; returns a NEW person, pure) В· `fldPersonTeam` (the EA-style {side,army,corps} journey hook) В· `fldProvenanceStyle` (the **Inferred-vs-Verified visual distinction** В§10 вҖ” Verified solid / Inferred HATCHED `repeating-linear-gradient` / Disputed dashed; meaning rides pattern + glyph [вң“/~/?] + word, NOT colour вҶ’ CVD-safe) В· `fldMusterHudLine` (the compact in-battle inspect line) В· `fldMusterRollHtml` (the full "Muster Roll" panel, ready for the journey-mode character sheet). **Data:** `musterTemplate` + `_r5Note` added to `data/ratings.json`.

Pure display; "" when ratings data absent вҶ’ byte-identical. NO new combat path; NO RNG.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (11 agents: 4 diverse-lens Opus finders Г— default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 6 raw вҶ’ **2 confirmed + 2 critic, ALL LOW, ALL latent**; 0 HIGH/MED; completeness verdict: no no-fudge-wall write, no determinism leak, no lazy-materialization breach, no escaping gap). ALL 4 fixed (defensive-copy hardening so a FUTURE bulk-person/career path can't corrupt canonical `GAME_DATA`): **(1)** `fldMaterializePerson` returned the AUTHORED persona BY REFERENCE (via `fldDerivePerson`'s authored branch) вҶ’ now shallow-copies persona at the materialization boundary; **(2)** `fldPromotePerson` with an unmapped/typo'd `toRank` silently mapped to the 64 anchor (a +16 unearned lift + false officerTier) вҶ’ now requires a real `rankBase` key, else a clean no-op clone; **(3)** the `sources` ARRAY was a second shared reference (and `fldPromotePerson` propagated it) вҶ’ now `.slice()`'d on both paths; **(4)** `fldPromotePerson`'s persona-less guard returned the input ref, breaking its "returns a NEW person" contract вҶ’ added `_fldClonePerson` (copies persona + sources) for every no-op path. ## D102 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q9**: the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE вҖ” promote В· multi-currency В· merit gate) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve, built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/political-capital spine + the R-5 person spine (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.2/В§14.3/В§15). The President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder, spending a **multi-currency** budget, **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display вҖ” **byte-identical until the player promotes** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Design law: В§12.
- **The ladder + the move (`src/35-command.js`, the "Q9 (D102)" block):** `_cmdBaseGrade` parses each general's VERBOSE `generals.json` rank deterministically down to one of **Brig. Gen. вҶ’ Maj. Gen. вҶ’ Lt. Gen. вҶ’ General** (the multi-word grades are checked before the bare "General"; an unrecognized rank defaults to the LOWEST grade вҖ” never invents a man up). `cmdPromote(C,id)` raises him one grade, spending BOTH currencies (gated on both): **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary вҖ” `capitalCost` by target grade, Г—`aboveMeritMul` if above merit) + a NEW **seniority** pool (`cmd.seniority` вҖ” `seniorityCostBase` + a `seniorityLeapfrog` surcharge when he leapfrogs a passed-over senior). Bounded, clamped, logged.
- **The merit gate (the honest history):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep вүҘ bar) вҶ’ a confidence bump (+`earnedRepBonus`); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) вҶ’ the capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation hit** (вҲ’`aboveMeritRepHit`). Because OVR = 0.55В·skill + 0.45В·reputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** вҖ” rank without merit doesn't make a good commander. (Teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence.)
- **How it reaches the fight (no new combat path):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small BOUNDED amount вҖ” `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase delta Г— `skillLiftWeight` 0.92), clamped to `skillLiftCap` 6 вҖ” added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating вҶ’ commandLeadership вҶ’` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). NEVER the scoreboard (D74/D94 no-fudge wall вҖ” `cmdPromote` mutates only `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation`). **0 lift when un-promoted вҶ’ every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical.**

## D103 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-6 (citation-provenance portion)**: the CATALOG-WIDE citation hardening + a permanent build-gate вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The R-6 increment's **negative-badge ASSIGNMENT to rosters + live dev-traits remain**; this milestone shipped the **citation-grade prerequisite** that gates them: every `Verified`-stamped claim in the data catalog now carries **вүҘ2 independent real sources**, the non-negotiable made un-erodable by the build. **A live violation was found and closed:** an audit revealed the debt was NOT confined to badges (the logged D98вҖ“D101 framing) вҖ” **47 records across SIX data files** were stamped `Verified` with <2 sources (badges 13 В· personas 2 В· weapons 9 В· artillery 9 В· engineering 8 В· terrain 1 В· cabinet 5). Outcome: **0 fabrication** (critic-confirmed), all citations real/on-claim/independent. The long descriptive forms ("Verified specs (вҖҰ)", "Verified (high) вҖ” вҖҰ", ~72 of them) cite inline in prose and trim-lowercase to вү  "verified", so they stay out of the structured gate **by design**. ## D105 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **LIVE DEV-TRAITS (the Madden development arc)**: a general's OVR now develops over the campaign, shaped by a hidden potential ceiling вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The last open item on the R-6 rating track (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§9-R-6: "reputation level-up вҶ’ OVR still TODO") + the D94-fork-#5 lock ("ReputationвҶ’OVR dev-traits = LIVE in-campaign now"). `cmdOnResolve` already evolved a general's reputation by battle outcome (decisive win +6 / win +3 / draw вҲ’1 / loss вҲ’4 / decisive loss вҲ’8), and `_cmdGenRating` (0.55В·skill + 0.45В·reputation) вҶ’ `commandLeadership` already read it вҖ” so winning a campaign already nudged his OVR. D105 adds the **Madden DEV-TRAIT** that SHAPES that arc: a hidden potential **ceiling** (how high he can climb), a **floor** (how far he can fall), a development **rate** (rise vs fall), and an **attritionDrag** (the В§15-R3 decline-with-heavy-attrition). **ACCURATE INPUTS, never an output gate (D74/D92)** вҖ” a dev-trait only shapes the general's REPUTATION (an INPUT the existing pipe consumes), it NEVER writes a casualty/winner. Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§9-R-6 / В§14.6 / В§15-R3.
- **The keystone (byte-identical-when-off, the R-6/D104 pattern):** the engine seam in `cmdOnResolve` is **byte-identical for an UNASSIGNED general (or absent devTraits data)** вҖ” it takes the LITERAL pre-D105 path `clamp(cur+delta, 5, 98)`, rate 1, no drag (proven across ALL five outcome quadrants + both clamp rails). The deliberate, citation-grade, historically-directed change is the AUTHORED `data/ratings.json` `devTraits.assign` map (20 generals вҶ’ one of 12 archetypes). The ceiling/floor are RELATIVE to the general's SEEDED start reputation (`devTrack.start`, fixed), every archetype keeps `ceilingAboveвүҘ5 & floorBelowвүҘ5`, so the pre-D105 "a winning general gains reputation / a losing one loses it" invariant holds for all.
- **The arc (in `cmdOnResolve`):** an assigned general's base delta is scaled by his `riseRate`/`fallRate`, plus a bounded extra `attritionDrag` when his side bled the lion's share (casualty SHARE > pivot вҖ” the D100 unit-correct measure), then clamped to HIS `[floor,ceiling]` band. New pure fns (`src/35-command.js`): `_cmdDevCfg`/`_cmdDevStart`/`_cmdDevTrait` (resolves the absolute band) / `_cmdAttritionDrag` (bounded вүӨ attritionDragMax) / `_cmdDevTrackUpdate` (pure observation) / `_cmdDevTrend` / `_cmdCareerArcHTML`. `cmdInit` seeds + sanitizes `cmd.devTrack[id]={start,peak,low,battles}` (rides the save, no `_SAVE_VER` bump). NO RNG.
- **The 12 archetypes + anti-Lost-Cause balance:** rising_star (Grant/Sherman/Sheridan) В· steady_rock (Thomas) В· established_legend (Lee/Jackson) В· natural_genius (Forrest) В· steady_professional (Meade/ScottвҶ’administrator/Longstreet/A.S.Johnston) В· cautious_fabian (J.E.Johnston) В· mercurial_cavalier (Stuart/Beauregard) В· administrator (Scott/Halleck) В· plateau (McClellan) В· overpromoted (Burnside/Hooker) В· volatile_aggressor (Hood) В· quarrelsome (Bragg). **The thesis is anti-Lost-Cause:** the Union's elite are RISERS (4 high-ceiling developers rated as high as Lee/Jackson вҖ” the honest claim that the Union found and elevated its best command) while command failures are named plainly on BOTH sides (US McClellan plateau / Burnside-Hooker overpromoted; CS Bragg quarrelsome / Hood volatile-disaster). All 20 assignments are stamped **Inferred** (a calibrated reading of a documented arc вҖ” gate-4e-exempt) with 1-2 real sources each; nothing laundered (Forrest's Klan + Longstreet's Lost-Cause slander named in the notes).
- **The read-out (`_cmdCareerArcHTML`, a new Command-desk "Career Arc" section):** the sitting general's dev-trait tier (label + glyph + polarity sign + desc), his OVR arc (startвҶ’nowвҶ’peak on a floor..ceiling band with start/peak ticks), a trend verdict (Rising/Holding/Fading/Untested) + the net delta, and a soft potential-room note. Triple-encoded (word + sign + number; glyph + colour decorative) вҶ’ CVD-safe; `wcag-auditor` AA (one nested-opacity spot 3.93вҶ’4.57:1 fixed).
- **The no-fudge wall extended (bug-hunt):** build-gate 4d (the no-fudge OUTPUT WALL) now also scans `src/35-command.js` (confirmed it writes ONLY command state вҖ” reputation/seniority/capital/devTrack, none in the forbidden set) вҖ” closing the coverage gap so the strategic rating code's no-fudge invariant is STRUCTURAL too (mirrors how D103's gate 4e made citations un-erodable).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (the ultracode pattern вҖ” 5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge В· byte-identity В· bounding/determinism В· citation/balance В· UI/probe] Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 29 agents; **8 confirmed + 3 critic-missed; 1 HIGH, 3 MED, 7 LOW; critic: "SAFE TO COMMIT вҖ” both hard invariants [no output gate, byte-identical-when-off] CONFIRMED HOLD"** via independent grep corroboration that `devTrack`/`reputation` are read by no combat code). ALL 11 fixed: **(HIGH, the only blocker)** a fabricated-by-misattribution Thomas citation ("Conquered into Liberty" is Eliot Cohen's, not Larry Daniel's) вҶ’ corrected to Daniel's actual *Days of Glory: The Army of the Cumberland* (CLAUDE.md non-negotiable #4); **(MED)** the Burnside note "proved right at Fredericksburg" laundered a Union command failure вҶ’ rewritten to name the futile Marye's-Heights assaults plainly (anti-Lost-Cause); **(MED, the keystone hardening)** `_cmdDevTrait`/`_cmdDevStart` consumed `devTrack.start` RAW вҶ’ a tampered/stale save (start NaN / 500) poisoned the reputation clamp вҶ’ now coerced through `_cmdNum` + clamped [0,100] at the read site, `cmdInit` SANITIZES the whole record on LOAD (the Q9 re-clamp pattern), and `_cmdCareerArcHTML` coerces the whole `tr` record (no "NaN" can render); **(MEDвҶ’the gate gap above);** **(LOW Г—7)** byte-identical-off probe now covers all 5 quadrants + both clamp rails; the off-test asserts `devTraits.assign` is restored (no global-state leak); floor/drag steps assert the locked general's trait; the render step covers all 4 `_cmdDevTrend` branches + the battles=0 edge; the new SAVE-TAMPER probe step (start NaN/500/вҲ’99 вҶ’ finite + in-band + no NaN render); the balance check counts named-failures as (вҲ’,~) so it doesn't rest on the single cs-bragg record.
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK В· no-fudge вң“` (4d now scans 35-command.js) `В· citations вң“` (the Thomas fix); `probe-command` **34/34** (9 D105 steps: data+balance В· byte-identical-off all-quadrants+rails В· assign-restored В· rising-star-vs-plateau+ceiling В· floor cap В· attrition drag bounded В· no-output-gate+devTrack-purity В· save-tamper В· render+4 trend branches); `probe-ratings` **21/21** (the tactical rating engine + the 9-battle badge resolution intact вҖ” D105 touches NO tactical code, byte-identical by construction, confirmed by `git diff`), `probe-desk` 13/13, `probe-camp` 8/8, `probe-officers` 15/15, `t1probe` 14/14, `bootprobe` ok; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors throughout; `wcag-auditor` AA. **ENV:** the 8 GB Mac had a healthy memory window this session; probes ran foreground via a threaded server (the documented load-stall gotcha did not bite). ## D245 вҖ” S25 PALETTE UNIFICATION: THE THREE PRE-BATTLE CONFIG SURFACES JOIN THE SHARED H0 --h0d-* TOKEN SET (PRESENTATION-ONLY, BYTE-IDENTICAL SIM) вҖ” [CLAUDE, per Aaron's D237 approval] (2026-07-04)

## D244 вҖ” E13+E41 SAVE HARDENING: THE TAMPERED-AUTOSAVE BOOT BRICK CLOSED (HOISTED OVERRIDE PAIR) + THE SAVE-SHAPE LAW GETS STRUCTURAL TEETH (BUILD GATE 4h + TRACKED MANIFEST) вҖ” [CLAUDE, per Aaron's D237 approval] (2026-07-04)

Aaron's approved pair, one gated code-health milestone. **E13 (the boot brick):** base `applySave` iterated settings with `src.hasOwnProperty(k)` (base.html:3159) and base `loadLocal` accepted a settings object carrying an OWN enumerable `hasOwnProperty` вҖ” so a tampered `gor_save` made the call throw at base:3983, which executes at SCRIPT-EVALUATION time mid-file: the uncaught TypeError aborted the whole script (every later declaration dead, game bricked until localStorage cleared). The D234 slot/import lanes were already guarded by `_slValidSave`; the autosave boot lane was the hole.
- **The fix вҖ” NEW `src/105-save-guard.js`, a D44-class frozen-engine override by REDECLARATION (manifest `overrides` += loadLocal, applySave):** the key insight is that the 91-save-slots reassignment-wrapper idiom CANNOT protect this lane (a wrapper assigned at module eval, ~base:14400, runs after the boot lane at 3983) вҖ” but duplicate top-level function declarations are hoisted at script instantiation with last-in-source winning, so the spliced module's declarations are the live bindings BEFORE the first statement executes. Verified empirically in-session and by the Opus panel (both base declarations at global top level; `init()` declared 3882, called top-level 4092; no assignment-form rebinding of either name anywhere in base+src).
- **Behavior:** `loadLocal` = base validation byte-for-byte PLUS reject own-`hasOwnProperty` settings (returns null вҖ” the tampered autosave reads as absent, exactly the D234 `_slValidSave` posture); `applySave` = same merge semantics with `Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call` iteration and the pollution skip-list extended by `"hasOwnProperty"` (sanitize: the shadow key can never land on `G.settings`, where base's own iteration would later call it). Byte-identical on every legitimate save (a JSON.parse of serializeSave output can never carry the key; no engine code writes it).
- **Negative control (default-refute):** the pre-fix HEAD deliverable served with the tampered autosave died at boot вҖ” `src.hasOwnProperty is not a function` + 2 cascade pageerrors (`TILE_SRC` TDZ, undefined `.failed`), whole module layer dead (no Save&Load button). The fixed build with the SAME tamper: 0 pageerrors, menu up, save rejected, `hasSave()` false.

**E41 (the structural gate):** the architecture law "save changes need a `_SAVE_VER` bump WITH idempotent lazy migration, or be purely additive" had ZERO build enforcement. NEW **gate 4h** in `tools/build.mjs` + tracked **`tools/save-shape.json`**: whitespace-collapsed sha256/16 pins on the 7 save-envelope-owning functions (base serializeSave/loadLocal/applySave/importSave В· `_slValidSave` В· the E13 override pair), a `_SAVE_VER`вҶ”manifest `saveVer` mirror, a required-core floor (the gate cannot be disarmed by dropping its base entries), a same-file duplicate-declaration die (the gate refuses to hash a dead copy), and an assignment-form rebind scan over every src module for serializeSave/loadLocal/applySave/saveLocal (importSave exempt: the shipped D234 wrapper legitimately uses that idiom and its accept shape is pinned via `_slValidSave`). Any drift fails the build with the computed hashes + the law text; updating the tracked manifest in the same commit IS the conscious bump-or-additive decision (the diff is the audit trail). Purely-additive fields riding inside settings/campaign never touch these functions вҖ” the allowed path passes untouched. **Honest coverage limits documented in-gate:** a brand-new persist path (different localStorage key) and the migration-actually-shipped half of the law remain review territory; the extractor has no regex-literal state (enrolled fns contain none; the realistic violation shapes fail closed on the unbalanced-brace die).
- **Fixtures proven in-session (all вҶ’ BUILD FAIL [5], then live tree green):** (A) shape-owning fn edited without manifest update вҖ” fails naming the fn + recorded/computed hashes; (B) manifest saveVer bumped without source bump вҖ” fails on the mirror; (C) core manifest entry dropped вҖ” fails on the floor; (D) `applySave = <expr>` appended to a module вҖ” fails on the rebind scan; (E) duplicate-declaration detection replicated standalone (second exec() finds the dup вҶ’ die).
- **Probe teeth (`tools/probe-save-slots.mjs`, 10/10 вҶ’ 14/14, no assertion touched):** a second navigation boots the page WITH the tampered autosave seeded (the pageerror listener persists across reload вҖ” a boot crash fails the artifact) + rejection asserts; a direct poisoned-applySave sanitize step; a legit-save round-trip identity step; a module source-hygiene static scan (exactly 2 declarations; the safe-iteration form present; no `_SAVE_VER`/`G.battle` writes). Two harness repairs rode along, assertions untouched: the probe screenshot got the 120s slow-Mac budget (D232 class вҖ” the 30s default flaked today under WebGL ReadPixels stalls) and `probe-full-campaign` moved off the stalling `waitUntil:'load'` to `domcontentloaded`+120s (the exact D233 class; it was red at HEAD today for harness reasons вҖ” goto timeout before any step вҖ” and is 4-steps green after).
- **3-lens Opus panel (default-refute): 3Г— SAFE_TO_COMMIT.** The override lens confirmed hoisting/load-order, byte-identity, and every consumer; the gate lens' coverage-floor MED was already fixed pre-verdict, its duplicate-declaration + rebind-escape MEDs were hardened post-verdict in-slice (fixtures C/D/E above), and its "cannot be violated silently" doc-overclaim was rewritten to the honest coverage statement; the probe lens confirmed the teeth are non-vacuous (triple coverage: reload pageerror + loadLocal reject + direct-apply) and that both harness edits weaken nothing. **One NEW pre-existing residual filed as ledger E50** (not a D244 blocker, outside the approved scope): `sv.campaign` applies wholesale and ~20 sites iterate save-derived campaign objects with the callable `raw.hasOwnProperty(k)` form (35-command.js:836 et al.) вҖ” a tampered `campaign.president.command.corps` still crashes navigation-gated command surfaces (never the boot); candidate deep-campaign sanitize for a future save-hardening slice.
- **Vetting (D160/D176 focused):** `node --check` Г—4 (module, build.mjs, both probes) В· build **GATE OK В· вҖҰ В· save-shape вң“** (new token) with the deliverable rebuilt В· **probe-save-slots 14/14 Г—2, 0 pe** (JSON readback) В· adjacents **probe-full-campaign 4 ok** + **probe-loot-survival 11 ok**, 0 pe В· `git diff --check` clean. (Reversible: delete the module + gate block + manifest, restore two probe lines; non-negotiables honored вҖ” base.html untouched, no combat knob, no RNG, no `_SAVE_VER` change.)

## D242 вҖ” E47 SLICES 3-4: THE SHILOH + GETTYSBURG FLIPS ATTEMPTED, HONESTLY RED, REVERTED вҖ” NEW PROPOSAL E49 (MASS-CAPTURE / STRAGGLER-COLLAPSE GAP); THE ARC PAUSES FOR AARON вҖ” [CLAUDE, per Aaron's D237 E47 approval + the never-push-red law] (2026-07-04)

The E47 arc's second half hit a genuine engine-design fork and stops cleanly instead of shipping red or weakening gates. Both flips were built, A/B'd, diagnosed, and REVERTED (the tree ends byte-identical to the committed D241 state вҖ” proven by a full re-sweep).

- **Shiloh (attempted):** `homeEdge {US:"low",CS:"high"}` A/B вҖ” default seeds BEFORE CS 7/8, meanCas US 10618 / CS 1131, atk/def 0.11 вҶ’ AFTER **CS 2/8 (probe direction gate вүҘ4/8 RED)**, US 4708 / CS 1464, 0.31; probe seeds CS 7/8 вҶ’ 2/8, 0.34. End-state diagnostic of all six US-timeout seeds: at the 480s buzzer the **US holds the Hornets' Nest corridor** вҖ” 3,108-15,755 US men ON the objective, CS ZERO in the radius, US hold-clock at 192-387s, nearest steady CS formation 153-445 yd out, CS ~23,000 alive of ~25k fielded (~6% loss). NOT the E48 buzzer class (Chancellorsville's CS stood ON the crossroads at the clock; Shiloh's CS genuinely stalls).
- **Gettysburg (attempted):** top-level `homeEdge` (T8 per-phase fallback) A/B, default seeds вҖ” **Day 1 McPherson Ridge inverts to US 8/8 (probe direction gate CS вүҘ6/8 RED)** (BEFORE: CS 6/8, meanCas 3001/972; AFTER: US 8/8, 2653/1993); Days 2-3 stay US 8/8; aggregate US 8/8 at 1.06. Reverted on the Day-1 red without burning the second seed set (the inversion is decisive).
- **The root cause (the D92 lesson, third time this audit cycle):** the E47 artifact was ACCIDENTALLY SIMULATING two loss mechanisms the universal model does not have вҖ” **mass capture by encirclement** (Prentiss's ~2,200 surrendered when the Nest was enveloped; ~3,600 Union prisoners in Gettysburg's Day-1 retreat through town) and **straggler collapse** (thousands under the bluff at Pittsburg Landing who never returned). With the artifact removed, routed defenders always rally at their own rear and RETURN, so a defense that historically dissolved becomes bottomless, and the two battles whose documented outcome depended on those mechanisms invert. Malvern Hill and Chancellorsville shipped clean precisely because their historical outcomes do not depend on mass surrender. Pre-flip Shiloh's US mean casualties (10.5k) approximated the real Day-1 loss by the wrong mechanism; post-flip (3-3.5k) under-counts it вҖ” neither is honest, and the honest fix is a mechanism, not a number.
- **Why revert instead of adapt (the laws):** updating the Shiloh/Gettysburg-Day-1 probe expectations would WEAKEN direction gates rooted in documented events (forbidden); shipping red is forbidden; keeping the flip only on Gettysburg Days 2-3 via per-phase homeEdge (the seam supports it) was considered and rejected for now вҖ” deliberately retaining a known-wrong physical behavior on Day 1 because it yields the right outcome is a per-battle fudge in spirit (D74), and it is Aaron's call whether that interim state is acceptable. **Filed as proposal E49** (candidate universal mechanics: envelopment-surrender + straggler-shedding вҖ” one rule each, no per-battle constants; recommendation: design session, then complete the E47 arc behind the same gates). E48 (the unanchored 480s clock, filed in D241) is adjacent but distinct вҖ” Chancellorsville's timeouts are mid-fall truncations; Shiloh's are genuine stalls.
- **State at close:** Shiloh and Gettysburg remain byte-identical to their long-shipped state (the E47 ledger line records the split outcome); probes green as of the D238 battery + D239/D240/D241 focused gates; the final full re-sweep on the default seed set confirms all 9 battles byte-identical to the committed D241 state.
- **VET (focused, D176):** JSON parse Г—2 В· build **GATE OK** Г—4 (flip, flip, revert, revert) В· A/B sweeps Г—3 (Shiloh both sets, Gettysburg default set) В· end-state diagnostics Г—2 (6 Shiloh seeds; the 5 Chancellorsville seeds ran in D241) В· final byte-identity re-sweep vs the D241 state В· `git status` clean (the two expected untracked docs/design files only) В· `git diff --check` clean. This commit is docs-only (DECISIONS/RUN-LOG/REVIEW-QUEUE/WAKE-UP/HANDOFF): no src, no data, no probe change.

## D241 вҖ” E47 SLICE 2: THE CHANCELLORSVILLE FLIP + THE ENDNOTE HONESTY FIX + NEW PROPOSAL E48 (THE UNANCHORED SINGLE-PHASE CLOCK) вҖ” [CLAUDE, per Aaron's D237 E47 approval] (2026-07-04)

The second E47 flip (data + probe tooth + one panel-mandated text-honesty fix; the seam shipped in D240). Aaron's live fair-gameplay concern this session ("doesn't this flipping home team thing undermine the alt history aspect? feels like we're tipping the scale") was answered with the panel's verification and shaped this slice's key call: anything that WOULD move outcomes beyond the approved rout-direction fix goes to Aaron as a proposal, not into the code.

- **The flip:** `data/chancellorsville.json` gains `homeEdge {US:"low", CS:"high"}` + `_homeEdgeNote` (the file seats Jackson's echelons at z 780-840 / CS reinf z 860, the US line toward low z / US reinf z 140-280; panel-verified the declaration matches the seating, incl. the XI Corps correctly seated forward at the exposed z 780 flank and now routing toward its OWN rear instead of through Rodes's echelons).
- **A/B (both seed sets, LOGGED never gated):** default seeds BEFORE CS 7/8, meanCas US 8280 / CS 2740, atk/def 0.33 вҶ’ AFTER **US 4 / CS 4, US 6244 / CS 5396, 0.86**; probe seeds BEFORE CS 7/8, 8009/2581, 0.32 вҶ’ AFTER **US 4 / CS 4, 6361/5350, 0.84**. The historical ratio is 17,287 US / 13,303 CS = **0.77 defender-pays вҖ” the post-flip ratio lands nearly on it** (the pre-flip 0.32 was the artifact: US routers annihilated inside the CS echelons). The 8 non-Chancellorsville battles: byte-identical to the D240 state on both seed sets.
- **The win-split finding (both panel lenses HIGH, all evidence logged):** every new US win is `by=timeout` at the 480s clock, and an end-state diagnostic of ALL five timeout seeds (7/21/33/303/909) shows the CS standing ON the crossroads at the buzzer (12,039-13,116 men inside the objective radius, US zero, CS holdSecs 88-133/140 вҖ” 10-52s short). So the 4/4 split is a clock-determined knife-edge, not emergent balance вҖ” but the clock is a shared unanchored template (480/140 verbatim across bullrun/fredericksburg/shiloh/chancellorsville) and any per-battle edit would be the exact outcome-engineering D74 forbids. **Filed as NEW proposal E48** (with the diagnostic verbatim + a recommendation: a universal position-falling-at-the-buzzer resolution rule over any clock guess) вҖ” Aaron's call, not a silent patch. ## D240 вҖ” E47 ROUT-DIRECTION FIX, SLICE 1: THE ROLE-AWARE homeEdge SEAM + THE MALVERN HILL FLIP вҖ” [CLAUDE, per Aaron's D237 E47 approval] (2026-07-04)

The first slice of the approved E47 arc (per-scenario role-aware home edges; Aaron-approved flip order Malvern Hill вҶ’ Chancellorsville вҶ’ Shiloh вҶ’ Gettysburg, ONE AT A TIME, each behind its own both-seed-set A/B + battle-probe re-vet). WHY: all four CS-attacker battles seat the US defender at LOW z while `fldHomeEdgeZ` was side-keyed (US=high z, CS=low z) вҖ” so a routing unit fled THROUGH the enemy line, inflating defender casualties (Shiloh 0.11 vs the historical ~1.2 attacker-pays) and reading as a near-costless Confederate assault: an anti-Lost-Cause teaching liability on the public game (D235 panel, ledger E47).

- **The seam (guarded, byte-identical when inactive):** `fldHomeEdgeZ(side)` (T0) now consults `__FIELD.homeEdgeZ` вҖ” set from a new scenario-data field `homeEdge: {US:"low"|"high", CS:...}` by `fldScenarioInit` (T1, single-phase) and `_fldBuildPhase` (T8, per-phase `p.homeEdge || top.homeEdge`, the attacker/defender pattern) via the validating `fldHomeEdgeSpec`; lazily resolved ("low"=-60, "high"=FLD.FIELD_H+60) so it always tracks the live FIELD_H; cleared to null on every launch (the T0 reset line вҖ” no leak between back-to-back launches, which the sweep depends on). Every consumer keys off the one function relationally (T0 rout/wavering-fallback/objective-press/defender-frame В· T3 officer command-post/ride-behind В· T4 supply-train rear В· T5 battery displace/cav flank-guard/flank-point), so the flip is coherent. Also role-aware: the two T5 no-visible-enemy fallback facings (battery, cav guard) via new `fldArmsFallbackFace` вҖ” face the ENEMY's home edge; the default path returns the exact original constants (US 0, CS PI) by construction, and in a flipped battle an idle battery no longer faces its own rear (facing feeds the flank-fire multiplier + the render).
- **NO-FLIP BYTE-IDENTITY PROOF:** with the seam built and NO data flipped, both seed sets' full 9-battle sweeps came back byte-identical to the HEAD baselines (raw per-seed results compared as JSON) вҖ” the seam is a true no-op absent the field.

## D235 вҖ” FABLE AUDIT M10: SIM-AFFECTING ACCURATE-INPUTS CORRECTIONS (C28 HIGH + C05-scale/C11/C30/C33/C43/C44/C47) вҖ” [CLAUDE, per D224 ledger] (2026-07-03)

The first audit milestone that CHANGES battle inputs. Law: D92 accurate-inputs / D74 no-output-gate вҖ” every change is a documented input (identity Verified, strength/count Inferred, sources named); outcomes were re-verified empirically on seeded headless A/B sweeps and the battle probes' historical gates, never forced.

- **C28 (HIGH) вҖ” the Gettysburg attacker/defender seating inversion.** All three phases had reused Antietam's US-attacker coordinate template without swapping roles: the CS attacker spawned ON the defended objective terrain (Hood at z410 vs the LRT objective z358; Pickett at z410 vs the Angle objective z295) and the US defender sat ~450 yd away at high z вҖ” the inverse of history, of the file's own COORDINATE NOTE, and of the three shipped CS-attacker battles (Malvern Hill / Chancellorsville / Shiloh). The file `_comment` documents the correction.

Seated correctly, the UNDER-MODELED Union defense collapsed (first post-flip A/B: Day 2 split 4/4, Day 3 CS 8/8 with the defender paying 2:1 вҖ” the charge walked in against the only 6 Union guns on the board). D212 continues Group 5 Phase H polish/media/perf without granting the M8 battle-build go/no-go. ## D202 вҖ” GROUP 5 В· PHASE H BASE 3D MARKER GEOMETRY PERF POLISH вҖ” [CODEX implementation + focused gate] (2026-07-02)

D202 continues Group 5 Phase H polish/media/perf without granting the M8 battle-build go/no-go. The slice uses the D201 Intel UHD-617 profile to choose a zero-new-media T0 resource/performance step: share immutable base 3D unit-marker geometries while keeping every material that can carry per-unit state independent.
- **Decision:** share marker geometry, not marker materials. T0 previously allocated identical slab/front/ring/pole/topper geometry for every brigade marker. Those geometries are immutable after construction and can be reused safely across unit groups. Materials are not shared because T18 casualty fade/routing opacity, side colors, flags, and selected/fading ring behavior mutate per unit; sharing them would risk visual-state bleed across brigades.
- **What shipped:** `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` adds a per-rebuild `fld3dUnitMarkerResources()` cache and uses its slab/front/ring/pole/topper geometries in `fld3dBuildUnits()`. ## D182 вҖ” GRADUATE-HISTORY PASS В· M3 RECONSTRUCTION/MEMORY вҖ” [CODEX implementation + source audit] (2026-07-01)

D182 ships the M3 Reconstruction/memory slice from the authorized graduate-history build-out. It remains a pure teaching/readout milestone, not a simulation or balance milestone.
- **Primary-source decision:** extend `data/primary-sources.json` with a new `reconstruction-memory` category instead of creating a separate Reconstruction deck. Rationale: the document-card contract created in D181 already carries the necessary `verbatimExcerpt`, `attribution`, `sourceCritique`, `indictment`, `sources`, and purity checks. Keeping M3 in the same reader avoids a parallel source apparatus and keeps quote discipline enforceable in one focused probe.
- **History-source decision:** the M3 seed set is deliberately narrow and load-bearing: Mississippi's 1865 Black Code apprenticeship law, Elias Hill's 1871 KKK testimony, and Frederick Douglass's 1865 "What the Black Man Wants." Each is `Verified` with вүҘ2 sources, a вүӨ60-word excerpt, and visible repository/locator notes. The Black Code record teaches coercive labor/restoration; Hill teaches Reconstruction terror as political violence; Douglass teaches Black suffrage before Appomattox as a condition of real freedom.
- **Amendment-date decision:** surface the Thirteenth as ratified Dec. 6, 1865, the Fourteenth as July 9, 1868, and the Fifteenth as certified/adopted March 30, 1870 while also naming the Feb. 3, 1870 state-ratification threshold. Rationale: Aaron's brief required March 30, but the codex must not falsely imply that March 30 was the threshold date.
- **Memory-manufacture decision:** update the Lost Cause codex to pair Edward A. Pollard's 1866 naming/Resistance project with Alexander Stephens's 1868-1870 Constitutional View recast after the 1861 Cornerstone confession. The card now explicitly teaches memory manufacture rather than treating Lost Cause as a vague later myth.
- **After-action decision:** the Reconstruction coda in `src/82-after-action.js` now names amendment dates, Black Codes, Klan terror, Redemption, Jim Crow, and memory manufacture. This is still a pure readout: no grade formula, ending predicate, combat path, save version, bridge facet, OOB, or battle-result output changed.

## D181 вҖ” GRADUATE-HISTORY PASS В· M2 READ THE DOCUMENT APPARATUS вҖ” [CODEX implementation + source audit] (2026-07-01)

D181 ships the M2 primary-source apparatus from the authorized graduate-history build-out: a new President's Desk **Documents / Read the Document** surface plus visible manpower debate-card scholarship. It is a pure teaching/readout milestone, not a simulation or balance milestone.
- **Source-apparatus decision:** the first deck lives in new `data/primary-sources.json` (`cw_primary_sources_v1`) rather than being folded into `data/codex.json`. - **History-source decision:** the seed deck starts with 5 Confederate self-justifications (Stephens Cornerstone, Mississippi declaration, Confederate Constitution, Hale to Magoffin, Cobb to Seddon) and 3 counter-documents (Emancipation Proclamation service clause, Douglass "Men of Color, To Arms!", Gooding equal-pay letter). It locks schema, excerpt word cap, `Verified` source count, Confederate catalyst frames, desk dispatch, filtering/search/expand, DOM purity, XSS escaping, and a static scan that tactical/bridge/save/output paths do not read `primary-sources` / `_ps*`. `probe-manpower` now locks the surfaced debate lanes and received only local-Mac navigation/screenshot budget hardening after harness timeouts; assertions were strengthened, not weakened.

## D176 вҖ” OPERATING POLICY В· QUEUE-LOOP GATES DEFER THE LONG AUDIT вҖ” [AARON clarification + CODEX docs] (2026-06-30)

Aaron clarified during the D175 queue loop that the repo must not run the long `npm run vet:noreg` audit after every queued item. The intended loop is to build the outstanding queue with focused per-item gates, then run the long audit once at the end of the queue/batch so failures can be fixed in one release pass.

- **Supersedes the ambiguous D160 shared-surface trigger during explicit queue-loop work.** Even if an item touches manifest, bridge, render, lifecycle, or suite enrollment, the per-item loop gate is: `node tools/build.mjs` to **GATE OK**, relevant importer/schema checks, `node --check` on touched JS/probe files, the focused probe, 1-3 adjacent probes based on touched surfaces, JSON/stdout/pageerror readback, and `git diff --check`.
- **Long audit timing:** reserve full `npm run vet:noreg` for the end-of-queue planned-work batch/release checkpoint, or for an explicit Aaron request. Do not treat it as a per-slice tax.
- **No weakening:** D176 changes only when the full battery runs. It does not weaken probes, browser guards, source-only editing, no-fudge/no-output-gate contracts, citation rules, accessibility expectations, or the ban on pushing red focused gates.
- **D175 note:** a full `vet:noreg` was started because older D160/HANDOFF/V1 wording still said shared manifest/bridge/render/suite edits triggered the full suite. Aaron stopped it; the run had passed through render-richness with no red conditions before interruption, but D175 ships on focused/adjacent gates under this clarified rule.

## D172 вҖ” PHASE I В· SIXTH CITATION-GRADE SOLDIER REPLACEMENT SLICE вҖ” STRONG VINCENT вҖ” [CODEX implementation + source audit] (2026-06-30)

D172 adds the sixth narrow sourced named-person replacement to Soldier's Story. Strong Vincent replaces the generated Gettysburg brigade-command slot `ss:gettysburg:US:us_vincent_bde:cmd` with a `Verified` sourced record. It changes `data/soldier-replacements.json`, `tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs`, `tools/probe-women-in-war.mjs` cleanup hardening, docs, and the generated `civil_war_generals.html`. It does not change canonical battle data, tactical combat rules, `build/base.html`, save schema version, item balance data, or Women in the War mapping.

- **Source decision:** NPS order-of-battle data places Col. Strong Vincent as commander of the Third Brigade, First Division, V Corps at Gettysburg. NPS Gettysburg material identifies his Little Round Top action, mortal wound on July 2, 1863, and death on July 7, 1863. American Battlefield Trust independently corroborates Vincent's brigade arrival on Little Round Top and frames Chamberlain's 20th Maine within the broader brigade defense. The record asserts no company, no regiment command, no brigadier-rank-at-battle claim, and no portrait.
- **Replacement behavior:** the canonical replacement pack now has six records, all `Verified`. The overlay preserves the 603-person registry, moves raw counts from 22 authored / 581 generated to 28 authored / 575 generated, keeps old-id alias lookup through `ssFindPerson`, and marks Vincent `Sourced` / `Verified`. ## D171 вҖ” OPERATING POLICY В· FRESH-CHAT EXECUTION GROUPS AND AUTO-CONDENSE BOUNDARY вҖ” [AARON directive + CODEX docs] (2026-06-30)

D171 supersedes the older "loop across the whole arc until context pressure" habit for current Codex usage. Auto-condense is treated as a safety net for finishing one already-bounded milestone, not the default project-memory mechanism across groups.

- **Boundary decision:** after every clean committed+pushed milestone, and before starting a new execution group/phase or browser-heavy batch/release gate, the agent should stop and return a paste-ready next-chat prompt unless Aaron explicitly orders same-chat continuation. If context is near ~70-80% consumed or the run starts depending on stale summarized context, finish the current gate, update handoff docs, and stop clean.
- **Grouping decision:** outstanding planned work is grouped in `V1-CHECKLIST.md` В§"Fresh-Chat Execution Groups": Phase I Soldier's Story scale-out first; GM follow-up leftovers; H0 batch/release gate; remaining Phase F/G non-battle systems; Phase H polish/media/perf; meta/deferred tooling; and the last battle-build queue. Chattanooga and USCT playable battles remain last unless Aaron explicitly reorders.
- **Prompt decision:** every handoff prompt must include `cd`, `git fetch origin && git status --short --branch && git pull --ff-only origin main`, current HEAD, exact next group/item, read order, queue locks, and the gate sequence. This makes fresh chats cheap and reliable while preserving the repo as the source of truth.
- **Docs decision:** the rule is written into `AGENTS.md`, `START-HERE.md`, `AUTONOMOUS-RUN.md`, `V1-CHECKLIST.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, and `WAKE-UP.md`, then logged here and in `RUN-LOG.md`. The change is process-only: it does not alter game systems, probes, battle balance, saves, assets, or source/data contracts.

## D169 вҖ” PHASE F В· DISEASE / ARMY MEDICINE WAR EFFORT SYSTEM вҖ” [CODEX implementation, focused-gated] (2026-06-30)

D169 starts the next non-battle Phase F content-system run after D168. The decision was to build disease/army medicine before the remaining hard-war, irregular-war, finance, diplomacy, named-unit, and human-cost systems because disease and medical capacity touch survival, manpower pressure, War Effort teaching, and human-cost gravity without creating a new battle or changing the combat model.

- **System decision:** add a War Effort disease/medical pressure ledger, not a hospital minigame. The system records sickness, wounds, treated men, disease deaths, and recent medical pressure from resolved battles; it teaches that disease killed more soldiers than battle while keeping medical organization as mitigation, not sanitization.
- **Implementation decision:** add `data/disease-medical.json` (`cw_disease_medical_v1`) and `src/63-disease-medical.js`, registered after POW exchange and before manpower. The War Effort overview renders **Disease & Army Medicine** in the existing overview/deep-block chain, wires a **Prioritize medical relief** toggle, registers `medicalInit(C)` and `medicalOnResolve(...)`, and adds a capped `medicalBridgeBonus(C)` to the existing bridge.
- **History/source decision:** existing repo source trails were sufficient, so no web fetch was needed. The data uses Verified side profiles and teaching beats for disease deaths, the Letterman evacuation system, anesthesia/amputation practice, the Sanitary Commission, Barton/Dix/Walker relief and nursing work, and the limits of nineteenth-century medicine. The framing rejects "clean war" and Lost Cause scarcity romance: capable bedside practice could not overcome missing sanitation, food, quinine, ambulances, hospital stores, or state capacity.
- **Bridge/save decision:** default inactive medical relief returns exact zero and leaves existing army facets unchanged. Only the explicit medical-relief priority can affect the bridge, capped at morale +2, fatigue relief 3, supply cost 2, and overall +1. Active relief can treat more men, reduce disease deaths, and mitigate Campaign Kit disease/fatigue only when that survival layer is already active; it never writes battle winners, casualty outputs, OOB, scenario data, or a scoreboard path. State rides additive `C.medical` with sanitizer/defaults and no `_SAVE_VER` bump.
- **Probe/tooling decision:** add `tools/probe-disease-medical.mjs` and include it in `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` so the future batch battery covers this D169 gate. `tools/probe-prisoner-exchange.mjs` also gets a screenshot timeout increase to 90s after a local 8 GB Mac false-red in screenshot capture; assertions were unchanged.
- **Gate:** syntax checks passed for touched source/probe files, including `src/63-disease-medical.js`, `src/20-president-render.js`, `src/30-president-shell.js`, `src/85-battle-bridge.js`, `src/90-president-register.js`, `src/99-h0-president-desk.js`, `tools/probe-disease-medical.mjs`, and the timeout-hardened `tools/probe-prisoner-exchange.mjs`. JSON schema smoke passed for `cw_disease_medical_v1`. `node tools/build.mjs` printed **GATE OK** and rebuilt `civil_war_generals.html` from source. Focused `probe-disease-medical` passed **8 steps, 0 pageerrors** with clean JSON readback. Adjacent probes passed: `probe-prisoner-exchange` **8 steps, 0 pageerrors**, `probe-logistics-rail` **8 steps, 0 pageerrors**, `probe-manpower` **9 steps, 0 pageerrors**, `probe-bridge` **6 steps, 0 pageerrors**, `probe-h0-president-desk` **3/3, 0 pageerrors**, and `probe-desk` **13 steps, 0 pageerrors**. Full `npm run vet:noreg` was not run under the D160/D161 focused-slice batching rule; the D169 probe is now part of that future batch.

This decision applies D145 to the main menu only; broadsheet remains appropriate for press, dispatch, editorial, and provenance surfaces.

- **Surface decision:** the first H0 surface is the main menu. Immediate H0 order stayed Aaron-selected: President's Desk overview next, then battle briefing/side choice. D164 later completed the President's Desk overview, D165 later completed battle briefing/side choice, D166 later completed the between-battle interstitial, D167 later completed tactical HUD/settings, and D168 later completed after-action/final report.
- **Implementation decision:** add `src/98-h0-main-menu.js` as a late assignment override for `openMainMenu`, registered after `97-accessibility.js`. The module keeps the existing button ids and behavior contracts (`gnContinue`, `gnWarDept`, `gnNewUS`, `gnNewCS`, `gnFree`, `gnSettings`, `gnLoad`) and keeps the existing injection anchors (`.gn-col`, `.gn-classifieds`, `#gnFree`) so save/help/playstyle/accessibility/tactical injectors continue to work.
- **Visual-system decision:** the H0 menu shell uses a dark command-interface layout with system fonts, status chips, brass/blue/red accents, panel borders, responsive three-to-one-column layout, battlefield imagery from existing embedded scene assets, compact badge controls, visible focus rings, high-contrast compatibility, and reduce-motion-safe transitions. It does not use `.gn-paper`, the broadsheet serif stack, or the old visible sword glyph treatment for the H0 shell.
- **Probe decision:** add `tools/probe-h0-main-menu.mjs` as the focused H0 gate. It checks desktop/tablet/phone responsive containment, no broadsheet class/font stack, command-grid texture, dark panels, polished injected labels, no old sword-glyph cards, visible modern focus state, core action wiring for Union/Confederate muster and free-battle picker, saved-campaign Continue/President's Desk path, pageerrors, and screenshot artifacts.
- **Gate:** syntax checks passed for the new source and probe; `node tools/build.mjs` printed **GATE OK** and rebuilt `civil_war_generals.html` from source. Focused H0 probe passed **4/4, 0 pageerrors** with JSON readback clean. Adjacent probes passed: `menuprobe` saved War Department path, `probe-accessibility` **25 steps, 0 pageerrors**, `bootprobe` `ok=true` with `realErrors:[]`, and `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`. Full `npm run vet:noreg` was not run under the D160/D161 focused-slice batching rule.

H0 saved-campaign assertions passed; the non-gating War Department screenshot capture can time out after the path is already proven open.

## D162 вҖ” PHASE H В· MODERN UG:G UNIT-ASSET SLOTS + FORMATION FIGURES вҖ” [CODEX implementation, focused-gated] (2026-06-29)

D162 adds a safe graphics/playability slice for the Modern UG:G battlefield: optional local GLB/GLTF unit asset slots plus procedural formation figures. It changes `data/tripo-unit-assets.json`, adds `src/tactical/T23-tripo-unit-assets.js` and `src/tactical/T24-formation-figures.js`, registers both modules in `src/00-manifest.json`, adds `tools/import-tripo-unit-assets.mjs`, `tools/probe-tripo-unit-assets.mjs`, and `tools/probe-formation-figures.mjs`, updates `assets/3d/README.txt`, adds the focused checks to `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` for the later batch battery, and rebuilds `civil_war_generals.html` from source. It also adds a timeout guard to `tools/probe-render-richness.mjs` so a stuck scene returns a clean failure instead of hanging.

- **External-tool decision:** the runtime remains local-files-only. The game never calls Tripo, never needs a key/account/credit balance, and never uploads or generates assets. Tripo site/browser actions, credit use, uploads, Generate clicks, or prompt entry require explicit Aaron approval. Canonical slots remain disabled until optimized local runtime files and clear license/provenance proof exist.
- **Source-quality decision:** canonical Tripo source slots require detailed/Ultra metadata: `geometryQuality=detailed`, `textureQuality=detailed`, `pbr=true`, `smartLowPoly=true`, and `ultraSourcePath`. Runtime files are optimized low-poly GLB/GLTF under `assets/3d/models/units/`; detailed source meshes are source art only.
- **Presentation decision:** when no enabled local model exists, T23 preserves the marker/fallback path. T24 adds procedural infantry formation figures on rich/high tiers only; `renderRich="off"` and low tier restore the slab/front marker. The layer reads render/unit state and does not write sim fields, call `fldRng`, or bump `_SAVE_VER`.
- **Probe/gate:** syntax checks passed for T23, T24, importer, focused probes, and the render-richness support edit. Importer passed with `records=8 enabled=0 detailedSlots=8 filesPresent=0 pendingLicense=8`. Build printed **GATE OK**. Focused probes passed: `probe-formation-figures` **16/16, 0 pageerrors** and `probe-tripo-unit-assets` **15/15, 0 pageerrors**, with JSON readback clean and screenshots captured. Full no-regression is deferred to the planned-work batch/release gate under the D161 batching addendum.

## D161 вҖ” PHASE F В· POW EXCHANGE CARTEL COLLAPSE вҖ” [CODEX implementation + source audit, focused-gated] (2026-06-29)

D161 adds the second bounded Phase-F War Effort system after rail logistics: prisoner exchange collapse, camp pressure, and relief prioritization. It changes `data/prisoner-exchange.json`, adds `src/62-prisoner-exchange.js`, registers the module in `src/00-manifest.json`, wires the War Effort UI through `src/20-president-render.js` and `src/30-president-shell.js`, adds a bounded bridge read in `src/85-battle-bridge.js`, registers init/resolve in `src/90-president-register.js`, adds `tools/probe-prisoner-exchange.mjs`, includes the probe in `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs`, updates docs, and rebuilds `civil_war_generals.html` from source. It does not reopen the exchange cartel, create a parallel campaign map, start Chattanooga, start USCT playable battles, edit `build/base.html`, bump `_SAVE_VER`, or add per-battle combat tuning.

- **Design decision:** POW exchange lives as a War Effort prisoner/camp pressure readout plus one explicit relief priority toggle, not as a second campaign subsystem. The module records detained, returned, and died-in-captivity estimates from resolved battle casualties and current year; the cartel stage moves from open to strained to collapsed through the 1863 USCT fault line and later camp-overcrowding pressure.
- **History decision:** existing repo source trails were enough; no web fetch was needed. The data ties the Dix-Hill cartel, Confederate threats and unequal treatment of captured Black soldiers, Lincoln's retaliation order, Andersonville, Elmira, and cartel collapse into one sourced teaching surface. The framing is not false equivalence: both sides' prisoner suffering is named, but the cartel-break cause is tied to slavery, Black soldier status, and Confederate policy rather than a neutral administrative mishap.
- **Bridge/save decision:** `prisonerExchangeBridgeBonus(C)` is exact zero unless the player explicitly enables relief priority. Active effects are capped (`morale <= 2`, `fatigue relief <= 2`, `supply cost <= 2`, `overall <= 1`) and cannot reopen the cartel; relief only mitigates deaths/returns and adds a small transparent returned-prisoner manpower boost when active. `C.prisoners` is additive and sanitized; no save-version bump.
- **Probe/gate:** the focused probe verifies data schema/provenance, default no-op, bounded active effects, resolve accounting, relief mitigation without cartel reopening, save-load sanitation, UI rendering/toggle behavior, and no tactical/classic contamination. Gate run: `node --check` on touched JS/probe files; soldier/women importer/schema checks; `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; focused `probe-prisoner-exchange` 8/8, 0 pageerrors; adjacent `probe-logistics-rail` 8/8, `probe-manpower` 9/9, `probe-bridge` 6/6, and `probe-desk` 13/13, all 0 pageerrors with JSON readback. A full no-regression run was started and passed every completed command through `probe-divergence` with 0 pageerrors, then Aaron stopped it and directed full-suite batching until planned work is built out.
- **Close-out rule:** D161 is resolved under the focused gate. D162 is not assigned here; it is reserved only for a Modern UG:G Tripo/formation slice after that slice survives its focused gate under the new batching rule. Tripo site/browser actions, credit use, uploads, Generate clicks, or prompt entry require explicit Aaron approval; runtime Tripo integration remains local-files-only and requires Ultra/detailed source quality.

## D160 вҖ” OPERATING POLICY В· TIERED VETTING GATES, NOT FULL SUITE AFTER EVERY NARROW SLICE вҖ” [AARON directive + CODEX docs] (2026-06-29)

Aaron directed this policy correction after the D154-D158 sourced-person replacement run made the full 80+ probe suite feel universal even for narrow data/content slices. D160 supersedes the D30/D61/D145 wording only on **gate sizing**. It does not weaken the hard invariants, source/doc discipline, or red-gate rule.

- **Always-required base gate:** start from live disk and `git status`; follow the source/doc read order; edit source/data, never `build/base.html` and never hand-edit `civil_war_generals.html`; run `node tools/build.mjs` to **GATE OK**; run the relevant importer/schema gate; run the focused probe(s); read JSON/output for `ok=false`, pageerrors, warnings, or fatal errors; run `git diff --check`; then commit and push only if green.
- **JS/runtime tier:** any JS/runtime change also needs `node --check` on touched JS/probe files and 1-3 directly adjacent probes. If the narrow slice touches shared seams, it moves to the higher tier.
- **Full-suite trigger:** run full `npm run vet:noreg` when touching shared lifecycle/manifest/build/save/bridge/tactical/render/accessibility surfaces, adding or materially changing a probe in the suite, or before a large milestone/release-batch push.
- **2026-06-29 Aaron batching addendum:** after D161's focused/adjacent gates were green, Aaron stopped the full battery and directed that the big suite stay disabled as a per-step requirement until the planned work is built out. The probes remain in the suite and must not be weakened; focused green slices may commit with honest documentation, and `npm run vet:noreg` becomes the batch/release gate or an explicit-request gate.
- **Repeated content-slice rule:** for repeated sourced-person/data slices like D156-D158, focused green + importer/schema green is enough unless UI changed, in which case add one smoke/Classic check. Run the full suite every 3-5 such slices or before the release batch.
- **Hard invariants preserved:** no generated/base hand edits, no per-battle combat fudge, no scoreboard/output-gate hacks, no save-compatibility break, no citation laundering or Lost Cause framing, no fabricated ranks/units/sources, no weakening probes to pass red gates, and no pushing red. `npm run vet:noreg` remains the full-suite command; D160 decides when it is required.

## D154 вҖ” PHASE I В· FIRST CITATION-GRADE SOLDIER REPLACEMENT SLICE вҖ” ELISHA HUNT RHODES вҖ” [CODEX implementation + source audit] (2026-06-28)

D154 adds the first narrow sourced named-person replacement to Soldier's Story. Elisha Hunt Rhodes replaces the generated Bull Run private slot `ss:bullrun1:US:us_burnside:pvt` with a `Verified` sourced record. It changes `data/soldier-replacements.json`, `SOLDIER-REPLACEMENT-FORMAT.md`, `src/37-loot-survival.js`, `tools/import-soldier-replacements.mjs`, `tools/build.mjs`, `tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs`, `tools/probe-desk.mjs`, `tools/probe-women-in-war.mjs`, `tools/probe-photo-embed.mjs`, `data/women-in-war.json`, the Rhodes portrait source/embed assets, docs, and the generated `civil_war_generals.html`. ## D149 вҖ” PHASE I В· LOOT/SURVIVAL HARDENING + GATE EXPANSION вҖ” [CODEX implementation + adversarial main-loop audit] (2026-06-28)

The first Phase-I continuation milestone hardens the D148 Campaign Kit instead of expanding its scope. It changes only `src/37-loot-survival.js`, `tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs`, and the generated `civil_war_generals.html`; no canonical battle data, tactical combat rules, `build/base.html`, save schema version, or item balance data changed.

- **State-machine hardening:** `lootInit` now uses safe own-property checks, rejects prototype-pollution/meta keys in `equipped`, sanitizes equipped slots before validation, caps saved `found` notes, normalizes survival turn sentinels, and cleans saved journey snapshots/logs into bounded plain JSON. `lootSurvivalActive` now requires literal boolean `true`, closing the restored-save/string-tamper path where `"true"` could pass the active gate before init normalized it. Stack additions now report the actual accepted quantity, not the requested over-cap amount.
- **Journey restart guard:** `ssStartJourney` refuses to overwrite an active Soldier's Story journey unless an explicit future caller passes `{ force:true }`. The visible Campaign Kit UI mirrors that rule by disabling Begin Journey controls after a journey starts. This prevents restart abuse while keeping the D151 persistence lane free to add an intentional restart/retire control later.
- **Survival tick hardening:** future-tampered `lastTurn` / `forageTurn` values no longer freeze survival updates forever; the tick/forage guards normalize future sentinels back to the current turn window before applying the once-per-turn rule.
- **Probe expansion:** `tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs` grew from the D148 MVP probe to a D149 adversarial gate. It now covers corrupted inventory/equipped/survival/journey save shapes, overflow and stack clamps, unique duplicates, actual accepted stack quantity, inactive and tampered bridge leakage, future-turn tick/forage tampering, save-slot import rejection for hostile settings, restored-save sanitation before use, full 603-person UI selector coverage, restart-blocking UI behavior, and a real Campaign Kit screenshot artifact.
- **Bug-hunt findings fixed:** direct main-loop audit confirmed and fixed the truthy-string active-gate leak, `equipped.hasOwnProperty` shadow/crash risk, raw stacked-item `found` notes, active-journey overwrite, and future-turn survival freeze. Follow-up static checks verified no direct `L.equipped.hasOwnProperty` remains and that the new probe locks the restored-save and screenshot paths.
- **Vetting:** `node --check src/37-loot-survival.js` and `node --check tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs` passed. `node tools/build.mjs` printed **GATE OK** and rebuilt `civil_war_generals.html` from source. ## D148 вҖ” PHASE I В· LOOT/SURVIVAL MVP + SOLDIER'S STORY PLAY-AS-ANYONE SPINE вҖ” [CODEX implementation + adversarial main-loop audit] (2026-06-27)

Phase I now has an additive Campaign Kit instead of a parallel economy or combat model. It ships rarity-tiered loot, a bounded inventory, default-off survival pressure, and the first playable Soldier's Story journey path. It reuses the existing R-5 prosopography/rating substrate and the Armory/Cannon rarity vocabulary; it does not change canonical battle data, tactical combat rules, `build/base.html`, or hand-edit generated HTML.

- **Campaign Kit:** new `data/loot-survival.json` + `src/37-loot-survival.js` + a `Campaign Kit` desk tab. `C.loot` rides existing saves as plain JSON: `inventory`, `equipped`, `survival`, `journey`, and `people`. Battle/campaign outcomes call `lootOnResolve` for deterministic rewards; the player can inspect inventory, use consumables, equip kit/weapon/keepsake items, toggle survival, forage, and begin a Soldier's Story journey.
- **Survival gate:** rations, exposure, disease, fatigue, forage, morale. Survival is **off by default**. `lootSurvivalBridgeBonus(C)` returns exact zero unless survival or a Soldier journey is active; active effects are bounded facet deltas only, never scoreboard writes or per-battle combat tuning.
- **Soldier's Story / prosopography:** `ssPersonRegistry` enumerates the current modeled game roster: authored rating personas, strategic generals and commission-pool figures, plus representative company officer/NCO/private rows for every current tactical brigade token across single-phase, multi-phase, and reinforcement OOBs. The Campaign Kit selector exposes the full registry (603 selectable people in the current build), not just the visible sample cards, so the player can start a journey from any current modeled person. Generated rows remain visibly `Inferred`; future work can replace them with citation-grade named bios/portraits/unit detail without changing the play-as-anyone API.
- **Reuse / no mutation:** person rows materialize through `fldMaterializePerson`, `fldPersonTeam`, and `fldPromotePerson`; D148 does not fork rating math. The adversarial audit fixed canonical-data aliasing so registry/journey creation does not annotate or mutate `GAME_DATA.ratings`.
- **Bug-hunt fixes:** stack-full inventory additions now return `stack-full` instead of false success; survival meter init preserves explicit zero values; the Campaign Kit UI now exposes all current registry people for play-as-anyone selection.
- **Vetting:** `node --check` passed for every new/edited JS file. `node tools/build.mjs` printed **GATE OK** and rebuilt `civil_war_generals.html` from source. Focused `node tools/probe-loot-survival.mjs` passed **8/8, 0 pageerrors**, including save-shape sanitation, bounded inventory, unique/stack safety, default-off bridge identity, active survival tick/forage bounds, deterministic battle rewards, canonical-data nonmutation, 603-person play-as-anyone registry coverage, and full-registry UI journey start. ## D147 вҖ” PHASE J В· CUSTOM SCENARIO PACKS AND MOD-FRIENDLY SHARE FORMAT вҖ” [CODEX implementation + adversarial main-loop audit] (2026-06-27)

Phase J's broader share/mod pass extends the already-shipped C4 Custom Battle Builder instead of creating a parallel mod system. Custom scenarios remain local/shareable data, not canonical historical battles, and continue to launch only through the explicit `custom_...` path. Hosting remains deferred; GitHub Pages can come later on request.
