The doc records the deliberate V1 scope: single-phase custom scenarios only, no custom `phases[]`, no per-battle damage tuning keys, and no custom ids in the historical registry.
- **Builder exports/imports:** `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` now exposes a template exporter, scenario-pack exporter, pack importer, and pack installer. The UI adds Template, Export Pack, and Import Pack to Slots actions beside the existing scenario import/export flow. Packs validate every scenario first, install only into empty local slots, refuse duplicates, and write nothing if validation or capacity fails.
- **Hardening decision:** the installer itself rejects duplicate scenario ids inside one batch, not just the higher-level import path. This closes the adversarial finding that a public helper could otherwise be called directly with two same-id scenarios and fill multiple slots with ambiguous local data.
- **Probe coverage:** `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` now covers the pack/template helpers, UI buttons, import-to-empty-slots behavior, duplicate rejection in both the import path and direct installer, forbidden combat key rejection, pack lookup through `fldCustomScenarioData`, registry non-leakage, no Classic contamination, and the unchanged historical roster.

## D146 вҖ” PHASE J В· SAVE / LOAD / SHARE HARDENING вҖ” [CODEX implementation + adversarial main-loop audit] (2026-06-27)

Phase J's save/share pass is now a hardening/probe milestone over the existing save system, not a new persistence architecture. It changes `src/91-save-slots.js`, adds `tools/probe-save-slots.mjs`, wires that probe into `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs`, and rebuilds `civil_war_generals.html` from source. It does **not** touch tactical/combat state, battle data, `build/base.html`, or hand-edit the generated deliverable.

- **Save validation and slot behavior:** saves are cloned and validated before import/load. The validator rejects wrong versions, arrays/primitive payloads where objects are required, `settings` objects that shadow `hasOwnProperty`, primitive/array `campaign` payloads, and stale/corrupt named slots. Named slot save/load/rename/delete remains localStorage-based and bounded to the existing save namespace.
- **Import/export hardening:** pasted JSON and file import now route through the same hardened validator. The visible file-import path no longer delegates to the base `importSave`; D146 adds `_slImportFile` and assigns a hardened `importSave` wrapper with an `_slHardened` marker so the base main-menu "Load from File" path is covered too. This closes the bug-hunt finding where file imports could bypass the hardened text path and reach base `applySave`, which calls `sv.settings.hasOwnProperty(k)`.
- **Menu and undo:** the Save Manager menu injection dedupes itself and reinjects after menu rebuilds instead of relying on a brittle one-shot latch. The one-turn undo path is deliberately narrow: it captures before `campaignAdvance` only for the learner-friendly accessible difficulty path, not Ironman/harder campaign modes.
- **Probe coverage:** new `tools/probe-save-slots.mjs` verifies manager API presence, UI labels, menu dedupe/reinjection, named slot save/load/rename/delete, export/import text round-trip, invalid/stale/corrupt/tampered rejection, `settings.hasOwnProperty` shadow rejection, hardened import marker, one-turn undo capture/load, and no tactical/combat state writes or redeclaration hazards. `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` includes the save-slot probe in the normal suite.
- **Vetting:** `node --check src/91-save-slots.js`, `node --check tools/probe-save-slots.mjs`, and `node --check tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` passed. `node tools/build.mjs` printed **GATE OK**. Focused `node tools/probe-save-slots.mjs` passed **9/9, 0 pageerrors**. Post-fix `node tools/vet-no-regression.mjs --from="save slots"` passed **51 commands**, including `probe-full-campaign` **4/4, 0 pageerrors** and `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`, `m3dActive:false`; probe JSON readback showed `ok=true` and `pageerrors=0`; `git diff --check` clean. Q5 Chattanooga and Q6 USCT playable battles remain LAST.

## D145 вҖ” MODEL ROUTING + UI/UX REDESIGN LAW + NORMAL NO-REGRESSION GATE вҖ” [AARON directive + CODEX docs/tooling] (2026-06-27)

Aaron explicitly directed this blocker-clearing pass before new gameplay work: update model-routing instructions, consolidate stale roadmap language, add a real frontend redesign milestone because the broadsheet interface is not the desired global shell, research a better game-like UI/UX direction, and harden the full-campaign probe into the normal no-regression gate.

- **Model-routing law:** the main reasoning/integration loop stays on the highest-quality model, specifically **5.5** for complex architecture, important code, user-facing text, historical judgment, UI/UX design decisions, accessibility judgment, bug hunts, final review, and irreversible/quality-critical work. Token-efficient helpers are allowed only for bounded packets where quality cannot be harmed: `rg`/search summaries, file inventories, probe-log summaries, mechanical doc syncs, exact-schema data cleanup, first-pass source gathering, and repetitive fixture/probe scaffolding. Every helper/subagent/workflow call must explicitly set model **and** effort. Smaller models never own architecture, combat balance, historical claims, UX direction, accessibility judgment, or final integration; they produce packets that 5.5 verifies.
- **UI/UX design law:** D145 supersedes "broadsheet everywhere." The app shell should become a more video-game-like historical command interface: brighter, rounder, more dramatic, icon-led, and centered on public-domain photos/illustrations where they clarify people/place/stakes. Broadsheet remains the in-world language for press/editorials/dispatches/provenance, not the whole interface. The redesign must preserve Civil War gravity, anti-Lost-Cause framing, WCAG 2.2 AA, keyboard support, `reduceMotion`, CVD-safe cues, no unclear-license assets, and the Intel UHD-617 performance floor. Research packet saved at `docs/design/ui-redesign-research.md`.
- **Roadmap/gate cleanup:** `V1-CHECKLIST.md` now has a real H0 UI/UX redesign milestone with target screens, visual-system requirements, probes/screenshots, and acceptance criteria. The Phase J saves item is corrected to hardening/probing over existing `src/91-save-slots.js` named slots/export/import, with undo-last-turn still open. D143's full-campaign probe is now part of the normal no-regression command via `tools/vet-no-regression.mjs` and package scripts `vet:noreg`, `vet:noreg:list`, and `vet:full-campaign`.
- **Docs synced:** `START-HERE.md`, `AUTONOMOUS-RUN.md`, `AGENTS.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, `.clinerules`, `.github/copilot-instructions.md`, `V1-CHECKLIST.md`, `RUN-LOG.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, and `WAKE-UP.md` were refreshed so the next run starts from the same routing, UI, and gate contract. Q5 Chattanooga and Q6 USCT playable battles remain LAST.
- **Probe policy decision:** do **not** remove probes from the universal scheme. The right correction is smarter harness discipline: focused probe + relevant no-regression/full milestone gate, JSON/pageerror enforcement, process-group timeout cleanup, and root-cause fixes for probe hangs. This audit found useful failures: accessibility's static scan saw comment text, `bootprobe` could hang after writing green JSON, `probe-phased-3d` could hang without a bounded failure, and heavy visual probes needed explicit budgets.

Final segment ended with `probe-full-campaign` **4/4, 0 pageerrors** and `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`, `m3dActive:false`. `git diff --check` clean.

## D143 вҖ” PHASE J В· **FULL-CAMPAIGN PLAYTHROUGH PROBE** вҖ” the owner-mode campaign now has an end-to-end guard from first battle to final graded report вҖ” [CODEX probe-only] (2026-06-26)

This milestone adds the missing Phase-J no-regression guard without changing gameplay. New `tools/probe-full-campaign.mjs` drives the live single-file game in Chrome and verifies the cross-layer contract that individual probes only checked in slices: campaign chain -> bridge auto-resolve -> `campaignAdvance` -> President's interstitial -> final D112/D119 graded war report.

- **Coverage:** the probe runs a dominant Union auto-resolve campaign through the full 31-battle US chain (`sumter` -> `appomattox`) and a dominant Confederate auto-resolve campaign through the full 28-battle CS chain (`sumter` -> `appomattox`). Each resolved battle must win, increment `stats.battles`, advance `idx`, add the battle id to `completed[]`, clear recovery flags, and surface the President's interstitial before the next fight. The final chain victory must null `G.campaign` through `warWonScreen` and render `#wwReport`, `Final Reckoning`, and `#wwMainMenu`.
- **Recovery branch:** a controlled Bull Run loss keeps `idx` fixed, enters recovery, sets `flipAtk` because the player lost while attacking, then a recovery auto-resolve consumes the flipped attacker (`bd.atk === "CS"`), advances to the next battle, and clears recovery flags.
- **Strategic-ending branch:** a mid-campaign `victoryReady="will"` state must surface the between-battles "The war can be concluded" offer and `pdConcludeWar`; accepting it renders the negotiated-peace framing plus the graded final report and ends the campaign.
- **Architecture:** probe-only. No `src/`, `data/`, build, combat, or save logic changed. The probe deliberately uses the existing `bridgeAutoResolve`, `campaignAdvance`, `openUpgrade`, `aarConcludeWar`, and `warWonScreen` seams; it does not invent a parallel campaign runner.
- **Vet:** `node tools/build.mjs` baseline **GATE OK** before work; `node tools/probe-full-campaign.mjs` **4/4, 0 pageerrors** (`tools/shots/probe-full-campaign.json` confirms US 31/31, CS 28/28, recovery, and strategic ending); `node --check tools/probe-full-campaign.mjs` clean; `git diff --check` clean. This completes the V1-CHECKLIST Phase-J "Full-campaign playthrough probe" item.

## D142 вҖ” PHASE H В· H5-i4 **FORTIFICATIONS DEPTH** вҖ” staged works, facing-aware cover, prepared abatis, charge impetus, and terrain sim hooks (the 4th step closing the locked D138 arc) вҖ” [CLAUDE impl, D74 gameplay carve-out] (2026-06-26)

The fourth H5 increment closes the UG:G-fidelity modern-engine push. Unlike H5-i2/i3, this is **not** presentation-only: it is a deliberate **D74 gameplay carve-out** because fortifications, terrain friction, and committed charges change player-facing tactics. The discipline is the D74 universal-model law: one shared combat/movement model, no per-battle outcome fudge, no scoreboard writes, and no AI-only hidden exception.

- **FORTIFICATIONS (`src/tactical/T13-engineering.js`):** entrenchment now stages from rifle pits / hasty cover to a full parapet to a redoubt/earthwork while preserving the existing `u.entrench` progress meter and B-5 realism scaling. `fldEngCover(u, fromX, fromZ)` is stage + facing aware: front fire gets full earned cover, flank fire gets reduced cover, rear fire bypasses the works. A unit that leaves its own works no longer receives cover while the visible works fade. The HUD names the stage and front-cover multiplier; 2D/3D draw hasty/parapet/redoubt shapes; the end card teaches the Hess/Mahan spade-to-fieldworks lesson.
- **PREPARED ABATIS:** abatis built by a brigade already inside its own parapet/redoubt is stamped `prepared`/`worksStage`, starts stronger, slows attackers more, inflicts stronger morale/disorder/fatigue shock, clears slower, and renders with a heavier backing + more stakes. A standalone abatis still works as before; prepared bite is tied to real works, not a free obstacle buff.
- **CHARGE IMPETUS (`src/tactical/T20-order-feel.js` + T0 seams):** player-issued charges get a 1.2s correction grace. After commit, casual move/hold/queue/re-aim orders are blocked until contact, target loss, fog loss, own rout, or own death. AI inline charge behavior remains unchanged. The HUD reports correcting/committed/contact status.
- **TERRAIN SIM WIRING (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** H5-i3's swamp/town/fort arrays now feed universal `fldCoverAt`/`fldMoveFactor` hooks. Fort = strongest cover + attacker ditch/parapet friction; town = hard cover + street/fence friction; swamp = soft concealment + major movement slow. Existing wall/woods/hill behavior is retained. `src/tactical/T22-terrain-readability.js` remains presentation-only; the sim reads live in T0 only.
- **Static guard updates:** probes and comments no longer describe swamp/town/fort as combat-inert in the live model. The D141 record remains historical ("visual-only in that increment"), but D142 is the point where those terrain arrays become active.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt:** direct audit found one confirmed bug: the charge-lock comment promised release on own rout/death, but `fldChargeLocked` did not test the charging unit's own state. Fixed `fldChargeLocked` and `fldChargeHudSelected`; extended `probe-order-feel` to assert own rout/death release and restored lock behavior before contact. Other audited risks held: AI charges unchanged, target loss releases, contact releases, no terrain read leaks outside T0/T22, flank/rear bypass retained, abandoned works give no cover, prepared-abatis scaling is bounded.
- **VET (PROPER VETTING, GREEN after the final fix):** `node tools/build.mjs` **GATE OK В· parse вң“ В· hex вң“ В· collision вң“ В· no-fudge вң“ В· citations вң“**; focused probes `probe-engineering-corps` **23/23**, `probe-terrain-readability` **29/29**, `probe-order-feel` **13/13**, `probe-bullrun` **15/15**, all 0 pageerrors; `probe-presets` **26/26**; `probe-phased-ab` **20 comparisons / 0 diffs**; full no-regression battery rerun after the last charge-lock patch **PASSED** (`bootprobe`, `t1probe`, core tactical probes, visual/3D probes, all current battle probes, and strategy probes); `diag-classic` reports **`nonBlank:346`**; `git diff --check` clean. Known tolerated harness noise: `bootprobe ok=true errors=10` with no real failure bucket and two `diag-classic` 404 console lines while the diagnostic still passes.

## D141 вҖ” PHASE H В· H5-i3 **TERRAIN READABILITY** вҖ” the modern engine now makes high/low ground (and every topography type) EXPLICIT (the 3rd step of the locked D138 arc) вҖ” [AARON 3 forks via AskUserQuestion + CLAUDE impl] (2026-06-26)

The third H5 increment: the modern (non-hex) engine's terrain is now EXPLICIT and READABLE вҖ” high/low ground at a glance, a player-chosen elevation render, an on-hover readout, and every topography type visually distinct. **Same discipline as i2 (NOT i1's carve-out): PRESENTATION-ONLY вҶ’ the FULL D74 byte-identity law** (proven via `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff). Hex = Classic, untouched.

- **Aaron's 3 forks (AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-26):** (1) elevation palette = **Viridis** (the reference CVD-safe perceptual ramp); (2) legend = **always-on compact panel** (docked bottom-right, collapsible); (3) topography scope = **add swamp/town/fort too** (not just name the existing types) вҖ” Aaron accepted these as VISUAL-now / sim-cover-wiring-later, which is what keeps i3 byte-identical.
- **WHAT SHIPPED:** NEW `src/tactical/T22-terrain-readability.js` вҖ” wraps the render seams BY ASSIGNMENT (fld3dInit / fld3dBuildTerrain / fld2dInit / fldPointerMove / fldExit; the T16/T18/T21 pattern, carrying ._wx/._atmo/._rr/._vf markers forward). **(a) Three elevation modes** on a new `G.settings.fldElevMode` ("hillshade" DEFAULT / "contours" / "hypsometric"), cycled from the T6 settings drawer + an `R` hotkey + the legend's mode chip. **HILLSHADE in 3D = T21's existing relief** (T22 adds NOTHING to the 3D ground in hillshade вҶ’ the relief is never double-counted); the 3D hypsometric tint (a viridis overlay mesh) + contour LineSegments+labels are PREBUILT once and `.visible`-toggled per mode (snappy, no rebuild, no camera jerk). **2D top-down had NO relief at all** вҶ’ T22 paints its own cached hillshade / hypsometric / contour layers (offscreen-canvas-cached, one blit/frame). **(b) Legend + on-hover readout** вҖ” a `#fldElevLegend` panel (mode chip, viridis gradient bar, a live elevation+type readout from `__FIELD.hover`+`fldTerrainH`, and a topography key of the types present this battle). **(c) Swamp / town / fort** вҖ” new render types read from `__FIELD.terrain.swamps[]/.towns[]/.forts[]` (each `{x,z,r}`), each visually distinct in 2D + 3D (swamp = wet teal disc + reeds; town = clustered buildings; fort = angular earthwork berm + bastions); a demo set placed in the sandbox showcase.
- **BYTE-IDENTITY (the i2 discipline, PROVEN):** T22 NEVER writes a sim field, NEVER calls `fldRng`, NEVER bumps `_SAVE_VER`. The new swamp/town/fort arrays are **combat-INERT вҖ” read by NO sim/combat function** (a static-scan assertion in the probe enforces it: only T0's `fldBuildTerrain` writes them, only T22 renders them) вҖ” so combat stays byte-identical despite ADDING terrain. The elevation mode is a new `G.settings` key the sim never reads (additive, the renderRich pattern вҖ” kept in `G.settings` only, NOT localStorage, so the documented "hillshade" DEFAULT holds every fresh session while the choice still sticks within a session + rides the campaign save). Proven: `probe-presets` **26/26** + `probe-phased-ab` **20/0-diff**; the sandbox COMBAT terrain (hill/woods/wall) stays byte-identical even with the new decoration вҖ” `probe-bullrun`'s golden snapshot was deliberately updated to the new intended terrain AND gained a `GOLD_COMBAT_TERRAIN` guard asserting the combat-relevant keys are unchanged (strengthened, not weakened).
- **VISUAL VETTING:** NEW `tools/probe-terrain-readability.mjs` (**26/26**) вҖ” 3 scenes (3D / 2D / low): the 5 wrappers + carried markers; all 3 modes render (hillshade hides both overlays; contours show a >0-vertex LineSegments + label sprites; hypsometric shows a viridis overlay whose LOW vertex reads darker than its HIGH); the toggle REVERTS; the legend + hover readout (hill crest `+yd`, swamp/town/fort named correctly); the decor group built + the key lists all present types; viridis MONOTONIC in luminance (CVD-safe); byte-identity (seed/sim invariant across a render burst WITH mode toggles, `errN===0`); 2D parity (all 3 modes run, `errN===0`); low-tier trims the 3D labels; a clean teardownвҶ’relaunch (legend removed + overlays nulled + exactly one legend); focus-restore on the legend mode chip; the legend key stays LIVE on a topography change; 0 pe; screenshot VISUALLY CONFIRMED (hypsometric reads high=yellow crest вҶ’ low=purple, legend + town + fort + woods all distinct).
- **DESIGN + BUG-HUNT (ultracode):** an AskUserQuestion design-note resolved the 3 forks before building. A **43-agent bug-hunt** (6 diverse lenses вҖ” D74-purity В· render-math В· lifecycle/leak В· perf/UHD-617 В· a11y/CVD В· edge-robust вҖ” Г— 3-skeptic default-refute + a completeness critic) returned **4 confirmed of 12 raw** + 2 critic-new; **ALL FIXED before commit:** **(perf, the keystone)** 2D contour mode re-stroked ~600вҖ“1600 segments individually EVERY frame вҶ’ now rendered ONCE into an offscreen canvas (batched to 2 strokes) + blitted, the shade/hyp cache pattern; **(a11y MED)** the legend mode/collapse buttons dropped keyboard focus to `<body>` on every activation (innerHTML rebuild) вҶ’ focus restored to the new control in the click handlers; **(MED) the legend topography key + height-range went STALE on a phase advance** (new sector, same-or-different hills) вҶ’ a topography-aware legend signature now refreshes the key on any terrain change in BOTH renderers; **(LOW)** dropped the localStorage round-trip (default-restoration + global-state concern); **(LOW)** removed a redundant double-dispose of the cloned hypsometric mesh; **(LOW)** the per-pointer hover classify now early-outs on a coarse cell; **(robustness)** the 2D ground hook (called from the base `fld2dDraw`, not a try/catch seam) gained a full-body guard so a render throw can never break the 2D loop. The critic independently confirmed combat-inertness, the fldExit dispose ORDER (T22 removes its meshes BEFORE the base scene-traverse вҶ’ no double-dispose), and the 3D contour orientation are all correct.

- **NEXT in H5:** i4 FORTIFICATIONS DEPTH (deepen entrench/abatis/redoubt earthworks + the charge-impetus commit-lock deferred from i1; this is also where swamp/town/fort could gain their sim cover/move effects). Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles remain LAST (Aaron's locked queue).

## D140 вҖ” PHASE H В· H5-i2 **VISUAL FIDELITY** вҖ” the modern engine now LOOKS better than Ultimate General: Gettysburg (the polished HYBRID; the 2nd step of the locked D138 arc) вҖ” [AARON 3 forks via AskUserQuestion + CLAUDE impl] (2026-06-25)

The second H5 increment: the modern (non-hex) real-time engine's LOOK upgraded to surpass UG:G вҖ” richer terrain relief, grounded troops, atmospheric depth вҖ” while honoring the period broadsheet palette. **This is the OPPOSITE discipline from i1's gameplay carve-out: it is PRESENTATION-ONLY, held to the FULL D74 byte-identity law** (proven via `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff). The hex engine IS Classic вҖ” untouched.

- **Aaron's 3 forks (AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-25):** (1) scope = **Max** вҖ” the full additive stack PLUS tier-gated 3D peg-ranks on capable hardware; (2) colour pipeline = **stay LINEAR + additive** (NO global ACES/sRGB flip); (3) ground relief = **Moderate**.
- **THE r128 DECISION (why ADDITIVE, not a tone-map flip):** THREE is r128 (0.128.0), PREDATING the r152 colour-management overhaul вҖ” no `outputColorSpace`/`SRGBColorSpace`. A grounded 5-agent recon proved a global `toneMapping=ACESFilmic` + `outputEncoding=sRGB` flip would SPLIT the pipeline (the T16 smoke + T17 precip ShaderMaterials write raw `gl_FragColor` and would NOT tone-map вҶ’ a visible seam: smoke darkens, rain warms) AND force re-tuning every hardcoded colour across T0/T10/T17/T18 for a palette that already reads period-correct вҶ’ EXCLUDED. Real shadow maps + MeshStandard/PBR terrain also excluded (r128 InstancedMesh depth-pass bug вҶ’ woods cast one blob; MeshStandard renders DARKER without an envMap under the linear pipeline; both UHD-617 perf sinks). The win is purely ADDITIVE, palette-preserving.
- **WHAT SHIPPED:** NEW `src/tactical/T21-visual-fidelity.js` вҖ” wraps the render seams BY ASSIGNMENT (the T16/T17/T18 pattern, OUTERMOST, carrying every prior `._wx/._atmo/._rr` marker forward) with five layers: (1) **ground RELIEF** вҖ” a slope-AO recolour of the terrain VERTEX COLOURS after T18 (height-relief darkens low ground / lifts crests, normalized to the battle's own height range, + a steep-slope exposed-soil tint + a small concavity term; latch `colA._vfAO`; positions NEVER touched вҶ’ units seat on analytic `fldTerrainH`); (2) soft round CONTACT SHADOWS вҖ” a per-brigade MeshBasic plane decal glued to the ground (a soft pool slightly wider than the block so the marker sits IN the field); (3) gradient SKY DOME вҖ” a BackSide MeshBasic sphere whose horizon tracks the live weather fog colour each frame (seamless ground-fogвҶ’sky) deepening to a richer zenith, + a free CSS VIGNETTE div (below the HUD, `pointer-events:none`, `aria-hidden`); (4) stylized rank MAP вҖ” a white-based CanvasTexture multiplied on each slab so a brigade reads as MASSED INFANTRY (CVD-safe luminance pattern); (5) Max-tier PEG RANKS вҖ” a per-brigade InstancedMesh of stylized pegs atop the slab (`!fldLow()` only), laid out once + x-scaled per frame (no per-peg matrix churn), with a bounding sphere so r128 frustum-culls it. Master gate = `fldVfOff()` (rides T18's `G.settings.renderRich==='off'` вҶ’ one toggle reverts the whole stack to the byte-identical default look). Manifest: T21 loads last among the tactical modules.
- **BYTE-IDENTITY (the i2 discipline вҖ” the INVERSE of i1's carve-out, PROVEN):** the module reads ONLY read-only render+sim fields, writes vertex COLOUR (never position), never a sim field, never `fldRng`, never `_SAVE_VER`. Per-brigade decorations are CHILDREN of unit groups (the base's rebuild/dispose loop frees them); T21 owns only the shared shadow/rank textures + dome + vignette (freed in `fldVfDispose` via the `fldExit` wrap). Casualty fade is correctly delegated to T18 (its `_rrSetGroupOpacity` traverses all children, fading the transparent pegs+shadow; `fldVfSyncUnit` early-returns on `!u.alive`). Proven: **`probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff** (final build).
- **VISUAL VETTING (the presentation analog):** NEW `tools/probe-visual-fidelity.mjs` (**26/26**) вҖ” 3 scenes (high/off/low): the 7 wrappers + carried markers; the BackSide dome (renderOrder -1) + its fog-matched horizon + the retained sky-background far-clip fallback; the `pointer-events:none` vignette; `colA._vfAO` + high-reads-brighter-than-low relief + positions untouched; the per-brigade glued shadow (gap ~0.5yd) + rank map + Max-tier peg IM (count 22, bounding sphere); the `fldLow()` peg tier-gate; seed/sim invariance across a synchronous render burst; `FLDVF_S.errN===0`; the `renderRich="off"` full revert; 0 pe / 0 texWarn; + a captured screenshot **VISUALLY CONFIRMED** (grounded units in soft shadow pools, the lighter-crest / darker-low-ground relief, rank+peg detail, the dome sky + vignette вҖ” a clear palette-preserving uplift over the byte-identical default).
- **DESIGN + BUG-HUNT (ultracode workflows):** a 5-agent recon+design panel grounded the r128 verdicts + the scope ladder before the AskUserQuestion. A 19-agent bug-hunt (6 diverse lenses вҖ” D74 purity В· render-math В· lifecycle/leak В· perf/UHD-617 В· a11y/CVD В· edge-robust вҖ” Г— 3-skeptic default-refute + a completeness critic) returned **SAFE TO COMMIT, 0 confirmed findings** (high confidence; D74 confirmed STRUCTURALLY вҖ” the headless stepper never enters a 3D seam). ## D139 вҖ” PHASE H В· H5-i1 **MOVEMENT & ORDERING FEEL** вҖ” the modern engine now moves & obeys like Ultimate General: Gettysburg (the FIRST step of the locked D138 arc) вҖ” [AARON 4 forks via AskUserQuestion + CLAUDE impl] (2026-06-25)

The first H5 increment: the modern (non-hex) real-time engine's PLAYER CONTROL SURFACE upgraded to UG:G fluidity. **This is the deliberate carve-out from the D74 byte-identity law** вҖ” movement/order changes alter the sim, so they are vetted as GAMEPLAY (synthetic-gesture probe), NOT via byte-identity. (The hex engine IS Classic вҖ” untouched.)

- **Aaron's 4 forks (AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-25):** (1) order model = **immediate + shift-queue** (a planned waypoint route); (2) charge = **drag-onto-enemy charges THAT brigade** (no impetus commit-lock yet вҖ” deferred to H5-i4); (3) facing UX = **point + facing handle** (tap places keeping facing; a drag swings a visible handle arrow; a moving unit's handle stays grabbable to re-aim); (4) fortify = **faster/cheaper digging**.
- **WHAT SHIPPED:** NEW `src/tactical/T20-order-feel.js` вҖ” the gesture resolver `fldResolveOrderGesture(sel, gst)` (the testable core: place+face В· drag-to-charge В· shift-queue В· re-aim), the waypoint queue (`fldEnqueueOrder`/`fldApplyOrder`/`fldOrderQueueAdvance`), `fldEnemyAt`/`fldOrderHasHandle`/`fldHandleHit`, and the live ORDER GHOST in BOTH renderers (2D `fldOrderGhost2d`: destination footprint + facing-handle arrow + stem + queued-route dots + charge double-arrow/foe-ring; 3D `fld3dEnsureGhost`/`fld3dSyncDrag`: a persistent group вҖ” ring + facing arrow + a charge foe-ring + a queue "+" tick). T0 seams: `fldOrderCharge(u,target)` (optional target; default = the VERBATIM nearest-enemy scan); `fldStepMovement` arrival вҶ’ `fldOrderQueueAdvance` (queue hook); `fldPointerDown/Up` rewired to the resolver + handle-hit; `fld2dDraw`/`fld3dInit`/`fld3dRender`/`fld3dDispose` ghost hooks; the HUD help line. - **BYTE-IDENTITY HELD FOR HEADLESS AI-vs-AI (the discipline that made the carve-out safe):** I changed ONLY the player control surface + the dig RATE. A pre-implementation Opus safety analysis + the bug-hunt's byte-identity lens + critic independently confirmed: no AI/scenario unit ever calls `fldOrderCharge` (the AI sets `u.order` inline), ever gets a `.queue` (only the player shift-drag creates it; `fldMakeUnit` never inits it вҶ’ the queue-advance guard is a strict no-op), or ever digs (T13 invariant) вҶ’ the queue/charge/dig changes never execute headlessly; the ghost is render/pointer-layer (headless runs renderer 'none'). **Proven: `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20 comparisons / 0 diffs (vs HEAD, final build) + all 9 per-battle probes unchanged.** So the per-battle sim outcomes stay byte-identical EVEN THOUGH this is the carve-out вҖ” the carve-out's room is the human's controls, not the AI's.

Left **UX-2** (select-radius can shadow a handle in dense clusters) as documented-acceptable for the 2-brigade sandbox вҖ” revisit with denser OOBs.

## D135 вҖ” PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") В· H1 increment 3: **PD USCT IMAGERY ON THE TEACHING CARDS** вҖ” famous public-domain photographs of the U.S. Colored Troops and their story now appear on the Codex cards + "The Ranks" manpower block вҖ” [AARON go (hands-off, edge-cases-only) + CLAUDE impl] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
**THE HANDS-OFF MODE (D134, standing):** the third NEW-asset category in the same "fully hands-off, edge-cases only" mode вҖ” I source/vet/embed PD imagery autonomously (вүҘ2 PD confirmations + period-accuracy + recorded provenance + a per-image VIEW), surfacing only genuine ambiguities. (3) `src/21-photo-embed.js` (NEW module, manifest after `20-president-render.js`) вҖ” overrides `window.portraitFor`: base hi-res relative-path photo (data:image/jpeg) wins when present, else this embedded 128px tier (offline-safe, framed by a pixel-faithful copy of base `_framePhoto`/`_photoMount`), else the base engraving (data:image/png); + a `.lead-badge` MutationObserver upgrade (the base observer calls the CLOSURE `portraitFor`, not `window`). The build grew 3.1MB вҶ’ 4.3MB (well within D34.4 "several MB; don't trade scope for bytes").

Proven by `probe-presets` **26/26** seed-for-seed + `probe-phased-ab` **20/20 (0 diffs)**.

## D132 вҖ” PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") В· BASE-ENGINE FIX: **MULTI-PHASE 3D SCENE REBUILD** вҖ” the live 3D scene now rebuilds when a multi-phase battle advances a phase (the new unit cast becomes visible, the prior phase's meshes are disposed, the woods/walls/objective-beacon move to the new sector, the camera re-frames it) вҖ” fixing a PRE-EXISTING base bug D131's bug-hunt surfaced вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The combat-path candidate Aaron chose (AskUserQuestion) over the H1/H2 external-asset layer (deferred вҖ” needs Aaron present for the per-asset IP/licensing review). **The bug (pre-existing, git-traced to predate T10/H1b вҖ” D131's bug-hunt SURFACED it, not introduced it):** the 4 multi-phase battles (Antietam В· Gettysburg В· Chickamauga В· Vicksburg вҖ” 4 of the 9 shipped) each run as sequential phases, and recon confirmed **every phase declares its own distinct sector terrain (own woods/walls) AND its own objective**. On a 3D phase advance the engine (`_fldAdvancePhase`вҶ’`_fldBuildPhase`, T8) swapped in a FRESH unit cast (new ids), fresh terrain, and a fresh objective, but **never rebuilt the live 3D scene** вҶ’ the new brigades got no `_u3d` group (INVISIBLE), the prior phase's groups + officer/supply/arms/eng meshes ORPHANED, and the woods/walls/objective-beacon stayed at the OLD sector. (2D was unaffected вҖ” it reads live state each frame; the headless sim was unaffected вҖ” no 3D. So the bug only ever showed in real 3D play of a multi-phase battle.)
- **EMPIRICALLY CONFIRMED FIRST (the prompt's requirement):** a NEW `tools/probe-phased-3d.mjs` drove each of the 4 battles in the live 3D renderer + advanced every phase exactly as the engine does, asserting the CORRECT post-fix invariants. Run against the **pre-fix** build it FAILED decisively (Antietam phase-1 `coverage=0` [4 units, 0 groups], `orphans=6`, the beacon stranded `dz=65` off the new objective at phase 2; Gettysburg the same) вҖ” confirming both symptoms (invisible new units AND stale terrain/objective) before a line was changed.
- **THE FIX (presentation-only; combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION вҖ” D74):** new `fld3dRebuildPhaseScene()` (T0), called from `_fldAdvancePhase` (T8) ONLY when `__FIELD.mode3d`, re-runs the same per-phase build sequence as `fld3dInit` вҖ” `fld3dBuildTerrain()` (fresh ground/objective-ring+beacon/walls/markers/woods/water) + `fld3dBuildUnits()` (the fresh cast; the T10 wrapper re-skins flags) + officers/supply/arms/flags/eng вҖ” then `_fld3dReaimPhase()` reseats the survey camera onto the new objective (B-6 side-aware). The scene-level per-phase terrain meshes are now tracked via `_fld3dTrackPhase` into `__FIELD._phaseScene[]` and disposed by `_fld3dDisposePhaseScene()` at the TOP of `fld3dBuildTerrain` (the renderer/camera/lights/scene/groups container persist; every unit-scoped builder already self-disposes). **The headless stepper (renderer 'none' вҶ’ `mode3d` false) NEVER enters the rebuild вҶ’ the sim is untouched.**
- **BYTE-IDENTITY PROVEN THREE WAYS:** `probe-presets` **26/26** (the difficulty/byte-identity gate); a NEW `tools/probe-phased-ab.mjs` headless A/B sweep (4 battles Г— 5 seeds Г— the committed pre-fix build vs the fixed build) = **20 comparisons, 0 diffs** вҖ” winner/winBy/per-side casualties/phase-score/per-phase-log/steps identical number-for-number (and historically faithful: Antietam CS-tactical, Gettysburg/Vicksburg US, Chickamauga CS); and all 4 per-battle outcome probes green (their committed expected outcomes are the pre-fix baselines). No combat/data/save file touched; no `_SAVE_VER` bump; never `fldRng`.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (6 diverse-lens Opus finders вҶ’ the 4 findings, ALL FIXED).** The finders returned **4 findings, all one class вҖ” a GPU-buffer leak the rebuild introduced by re-calling builders that weren't self-disposing:** **(HIGH + MED, same bug)** `fld3dBuildEng` (T13) did a bare `parent.remove(_engGroup)` (detach WITHOUT traverse-disposing) then dropped the mesh refs вҶ’ a phase with entrenchments/abatis/pontoons (the Vicksburg siege) orphaned their geometries/materials on every advance, and the detached group escaped `fld3dDispose`'s scene-traverse at exit too вҶ’ **FIXED** self-disposing (`_fld3dDisposeGroup(_engGroup)` first вҖ” the berm/abatis/pontoon meshes are its children вҖ” matching every other builder; does NOT touch water); **(MED)** `fld3dBuildWater` (T13) disposed its prior `_waterGroup` only AFTER the no-river early-return вҶ’ a riverвҶ’no-river phase advance left a stale + leaked river вҶ’ **FIXED** by moving the dispose ABOVE the early-return; **(LOW)** the T8 rebuild call site fully swallowed exceptions, masking the very invisible-brigade failure D132 fixes вҶ’ **FIXED** to `console.warn` (a real failure now surfaces + a probe's console gate catches it; the phase still advances). A **completeness self-check** then confirmed EVERY builder `fld3dRebuildPhaseScene` calls now self-disposes (terrain via `_phaseScene`, markers/beacon tracked, units/officers/supply/arms self-dispose, flags idempotent, eng + water now self-dispose) вҶ’ the leak surface is fully closed. (The hunt's automated verify+critic legs were env-blocked вҖ” a hung 6th finder + an OOM on the 8 GB Mac during the focused re-run вҖ” so they were substituted by inline code-verification of all 4 findings + a standalone completeness-critic agent + the empirical re-vet, the D124/D128 substitution precedent.)
- **Re-vet after the fixes (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-phased-3d` **64/64** (all 4 battles, every phase: coverage=1 В· 0 orphans В· groupsChildren==units В· the beacon re-seats on the new objective at every phase В· woods rebuilt per sector В· non-blank render В· 0 pageerrors В· 0 texture warnings) вҖ” re-confirmed AFTER the T13 fixes; `probe-presets` **26/26** re-confirmed post-fix; `probe-phased-ab` **20/20 0 diffs**; `probe-atmospherics` 18/18 В· `probe-weather` 30/30 В· `probe-render-richness` 30/30 В· `probe-audio-ambience` 22/22 В· `probe-flags` 36/36 В· `probe-tactical-visuals` 10/10 (the atmospheric/flag stack coexists); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` ok; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; VISUALLY CONFIRMED (the captured Burnside's-Bridge phase-2 shot now shows the fresh sector + visible brigades + the re-seated beacon under T17's dawn fog вҖ” previously empty). `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction (no new DOM/UI вҖ” only a camera re-aim + 3D mesh rebuild). **ENV:** `probe-engineering`/`probe-engineering-corps` are `waitUntil:'load'` вҶ’ blocked by the documented THREE-CDN headless load-stall (D97/D110), NOT a regression вҖ” the eng/water 3D builders are instead exercised by the `domcontentloaded` `probe-phased-3d` (which drives them through 12 phase advances) + `probe-tactical-visuals`. **Committed + pushed only after the full empirical gate passed.** (Reversible; non-negotiables honored: D74 combat byte-identity proven 3 ways В· the empirical-vet-before-push gate В· base.html untouched.)

## D131 вҖ” PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") В· H1b: **FLAGS & INSIGNIA DEEPENING** вҖ” citation-grade battle-aware flag selection + corrected Kearny-patch corps-badge SHAPES (date-gated to the 1863 fields) drawn on the 2D/3D unit markers + the selected-brigade HUD, DEEPENING the existing `src/tactical/T10-flags.js` вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The H1b increment per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 5 + memory `civilwar-idea-brigade-battle-flags`. **`T10-flags.js` ALREADY existed** (a basic flag/insignia layer shipped earlier) вҶ’ H1b DEEPENS it (the D91 deepen-not-replace ethic); it does NOT add a new module. Recon of the prior code found **three real defects, all fixed here:** (1) the 2D path computed an SVG + a `new Image()` it NEVER drew вҶ’ 2D flags rendered as blank solid-colour rectangles; (2) corps-badge SHAPES were never drawn (only a text label), and the shape MAP was wrong вҖ” II Corps was a circle (should be a TREFOIL), V and VI were both a generic "cross"; (3) corps badges showed on ALL battles regardless of date (an anachronism on the 1861-62 fields), and a roman-numeral substring match mis-read "II Corps" as "I Corps".
- **What shipped (the deepening):** (1) **battle-AWARE flag selection** вҖ” a new `_FLD_BATTLE_META` table (date/theater/badge-eligibility per scenario) drives the Confederate "default" flag: **First National "Stars and Bars"** at First Bull Run (the ANV battle flag did NOT exist on 21 Jul 1861 вҖ” its very creation was prompted by the smoke-confusion of the Stars and Bars with the U.S. flag THAT day) and in the early West (Shiloh), the **ANV battle flag (Southern Cross)** for the mid-war East, the **Hardee pattern** (blue field + white disc) for the native Army of Tennessee, with **Longstreet's transferred Eastern brigades (Hood/Kershaw/Law) flying the ANV flag even at Chickamauga**; (2) **NEW flag patterns drawn for real** (the doc once claimed an unimplemented "hardee") вҖ” first-national, hardee, polk (upright St-George cross, distinct from the ANV diagonal saltire), and a US cavalry guidon, all procedural canvas; (3) **corrected Kearny-patch corps-badge SHAPES drawn as glyphs** вҖ” I=disc, II=trefoil, III=diamond, V=Maltese (a flared cross pattГ©e), VI=Greek cross (plain, distinct from V), XI=crescent, XII=star вҖ” coloured by division (1st=red/2nd=white/3rd=blue) and ALWAYS paired with a text label (CVD-safe: shape + label, never colour alone), with a light parchment **halo** so the shape silhouette reads on any background; (4) the **anachronism GATE** вҖ” badges (adopted by Hooker's Circular of 21 Mar 1863) appear ONLY at the Eastern post-Mar-1863 fields (here Chancellorsville + Gettysburg) and NEVER on Bull Run / Malvern Hill / Antietam / Fredericksburg (where the corps existed but wore no badge yet вҖ” the HUD names the adoption date there as a teaching beat); (5) a **working 2D draw** (a cached canvas blit, fog-gated) + a deepened **HUD** (the flag thumbnail + the badge swatch + a citation-grade provenance caption).
- **CITATION-GRADE CONTENT (a research+verify Workflow, 25 agents: 6 Opus historian-finders Г— 3-lens default-refute verifiers + a synthesis):** the verified fact-sheet CONFIRMED the core code and surfaced two refinements I applied вҖ” the **Chickamauga ANV-transplant split** (Hood/Kershaw were Longstreet's Eastern divisions, ANV flag) and **Vicksburg** flying a Western pattern (Pemberton's Western-lineage army), not the Eastern ANV cross вҖ” plus a doc-citation softening ("General Orders No. 53" вҶ’ "Hooker's Circular of 21 March 1863"; the surviving primary artifact is a Headquarters AotP circular, the No. 53 label under-attested; the DATE is solid). вүҘ2 independent reputable sources per flag/badge/date (Encyclopedia Virginia В· Smithsonian NMAH В· Britannica В· confederateflags.org В· Tennessee State Museum В· crwflags.com FOTW В· Washington Times В· Gettysburg Flag Works В· American Battlefield Trust), anti-Lost-Cause (the battle flag's origin framed factually as a post-Manassas battlefield-recognition device, not romanticized).
- **ARCHITECTURE вҖ” combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. The render fns (`fldDrawFlags` 2D / `fld3dBuildFlags` 3D / `fldFlagHudSelected` HUD) are reached only through the EXISTING T0 `typeof` seams (probes drive the sim headlessly and never call them). Reads sim state READ-ONLY (`u.name/side/x/z/facing/alive/state`, `__FIELD.scenario/fog/units`) + `G.settings`; writes NO sim field, NEVER calls `fldRng`, bumps no save-version. The install block wraps ONLY `fld3dBuildUnits`/`fld3dDispose` (disposal of flag+corps-badge CanvasTextures, + a reinforcement re-skin) via a generic `_fldFlagKeep` that propagates any prior introspection markers (the D130 lesson) вҖ” these are NOT the T16/T17/T18/T19 marker-bearing fns, so no chain is shadowed (probe-confirmed the `._atmo`/`._wx` chain stays intact). Diff = `src/tactical/T10-flags.js` (deepened) + `tools/probe-flags.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. **No combat / data / save file touched** вҶ’ all 9 battles byte-identical seed-for-seed (probe-presets 26/26).
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern вҖ” 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity В· fog-leak В· history/Lost-Cause В· robustness В· perf/GPU В· a11y/DOM] Г— 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 46 agents; critic confidence HIGH).** **1 CONFIRMED finding (3/3) + 6 critic areas вҶ’ 3 in-scope fixes applied, 1 base bug SURFACED, 2 noted:** **(CONFIRMED, MED вҖ” a PRE-EXISTING base T0/T8 bug, git-traced to predate T10 вҶ’ SURFACED, NOT fixed in this presentation-only milestone):** a phased-battle 3D phase-advance (`_fldBuildPhase`/`_fldAdvancePhase` in the combat-path T8) swaps in new unit ids but never rebuilds the `_u3d` 3D groups вҶ’ new-phase units get no 3D group + the prior phase's groups orphan; H1b only marginally enlarges the orphaned-mesh footprint by adding CanvasTextures. Fixing it touches the combat path (byte-identity risk) and belongs in a dedicated T0/T8 pass вҖ” recommended fix: call `fld3dBuildUnits()`+`fld3dBuildFlags()` from `_fldAdvancePhase` when `mode3d`. **(IN-SCOPE FIXES, all applied + re-vetted):** (a) a **reinforcement re-skin** вҖ” the `fld3dBuildUnits` wrapper now re-runs `fld3dBuildFlags` after the base rebuild so REINFORCEMENT arrivals (Bull Run's late brigades) also fly the proper textured flag + badge instead of the base plain-colour plane; (b) a **badge silhouette halo** вҖ” a dark 3rd-division-blue badge on the dark HUD read poorly вҶ’ a light parchment halo now lifts every badge shape off any background (the CVD shape cue stays legible); (c) **fog-gate probe coverage** вҖ” the most-emphasized contract was untested вҶ’ probe-flags now exercises a fog scene (fog conceals вүҘ1 enemy; every hidden enemy's group is invisible so its flag + badge never betray it) + a static-scan of the 2D guard. **NOTED for future H1b polish (niceties, not bugs):** batteries fly a brigade flag (artillery carried guidons); the US-guidon / CS-cavalry asymmetry. The robustness / XSS / a11y lenses were clean (no raw unit name is injected into the HUD; all dict iterations are `hasOwnProperty`-guarded; the roman parse + division lookups are integer-keyed).
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK В· no-fudge вң“ В· citations вң“`; `probe-flags` **36/36** (battle-aware flags В· the date gate В· corrected shapes II=trefoil + V/VI distinct В· roman parse never mis-reads IIвҶ’I В· division colours В· CS-never-badged В· the Chickamauga split + Vicksburg Western flag В· CVD-safe HUD + the Mar-1863 teaching note В· live 3D textured flags + badge meshes on Gettysburg В· the Antietam gate builds NO badge mesh В· **fog-of-war: no flag/badge betrays a hidden enemy** В· byte-identity: sim seed + fields invariant across a 200-frame burst В· 0 tex warnings В· 0 pe); `probe-presets` **26/26** (byte-identity вҶ’ **combat byte-identical**, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` **18/18** (T16) / `probe-weather` **30/30** (T17) / `probe-render-richness` **30/30** (T18) / `probe-audio-ambience` **22/22** (T19) вҖ” all coexist; `probe-tactical-visuals` **10/10** (0 texture warnings); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 14/14; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`. `wcag-auditor` AA вҖ” the new HUD DOM passes by construction (every text colour clears 4.5:1 by a wide margin, the img border clears 3:1, alt text present, CVD shape+label) вҶ’ no changes. **NEXT in H:** H1/H2 PD imagery + reenactment footage (**SURFACE first** вҖ” external assets / network / IP / single-file stress; an external-audio-file layer is the same kind of fork вҶ’ SURFACE first) вҶ’ a per-phase-weather candidate (Antietam dawn-fogвҶ’afternoon via `_fldPhaseView`, a combat-path file вҶ’ prove byte-identity) вҶ’ and the discovered **phased-3D base bug** as a dedicated base-engine fix. **Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles LAST** (Aaron's locked queue). ## D130 вҖ” PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") В· H4: **BATTLE-AMBIENCE AUDIO DEEPENING** вҖ” a default-OFF, opt-in, stereo-spatialized procedural battle-soundscape bed (rolling-fire wash + gated cannonade sub-bass + fog-gated located cannon/musket reports) UNDER the existing T9 din+SFX вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-25)
The H4 increment per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 4 + the D91 "continue audio incrementally" decision. The base.html `dinSet` din already gives a MONO intensity bed (rumble + cannon thump + musket crackle), and T9-audio.js (D77) bridges it into the modern tactical engine. H4 DEEPENS the subsystem with a NEW layer вҖ” it does NOT replace T9. **Sub-choice decided-&-logged:** a NEW `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` module (the T16/T17/T18 wrap-by-assignment precedent) rather than editing T9 in place вҖ” lowest-risk, idiomatic, keeps the SFX bridge intact. PROCEDURAL WebAudio synthesis only ($0 / single-file вҖ” no external sound files; the linked-asset audio fork remains un-started + would be SURFACED first).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` вҖ” a spatialized "great-battle" bed layered UNDER T9's din+SFX, pairing 1:1 with the T16 gunsmoke (sound comes from where the smoke rises): (1) a continuous **rolling-fire wash** (looping band-passed noise + a slow swell-LFO tremolo, gain tracking battle intensity вҖ” the "one continuous roar"); (2) a **cannonade sub-bass rumble** (looping low-passed brown noise, gated up by the count of brigades actually working their guns); (3) **located cannon/musket reports** вҖ” a cannon = sharp crack + body thump + rolling reverberant tail; a musket = a filtered-noise volley "rip" вҖ” each panned in stereo by the firing brigade's field-x (side-corrected to the camera end) and **fog-gated** (a hidden foe makes no located sound). Discoverable via a new accessible "Battle ambience" On/Off row appended to T9's audio panel; one-time captioned through T9's accessible caption.
- **ARCHITECTURE вҖ” combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dRender` / `fld2dDraw` (drive the per-frame decision tick, throttled) / `fldExit` (dispose) / T9's `_fldAudioPanelRows` (append the toggle row) BY ASSIGNMENT вҖ” with a generic `keep()` helper that propagates EVERY prior introspection marker (`._atmo`/`._wx`/`._t9audio`/T18's) onto each new wrapper so the sibling probes still see the chain (a regression the no-regression sweep caught mid-build вҖ” fixed before commit). OWNS a separate AudioContext (the AUDIO_SCORE / SOUND one-context-per-subsystem convention). Reads ONLY render + read-only sim fields (`u._artFlash`/`u.targetId`/`u.ammo`/`u.state`/`u.x`/`u.id`/`u.side`/`u.alive`, `__FIELD.phase/paused/fog/units`) + `G.settings`; writes NO sim field, NEVER calls `fldRng` (no randomness reaches the sim вҖ” audio texture uses `Math.random` like base.html's din), no `_SAVE_VER` (the `battleAmbience` flag is lazy-defaulted). The SCHEDULING DECISIONS (intensity, fog-gate, pan) are recorded in a `FLDAMB` state object whether or not a real audio device exists вҶ’ fully testable headless. Diff = `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T19 after T18) + `tools/probe-audio-ambience.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. Proven by `probe-presets` 26/26 byte-identity AND a per-pure-render-window sim-seed-invariance assertion (240Г— `fldAmbUpdate`, seed unmoved).
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** **DEFAULT-OFF** (`G.settings.battleAmbience !== true` вҶ’ zero sound, never built вҖ” the byte-identical-mix default), **fully suppressed under `reduceMotion`** (the calm default вҖ” the T16 convention), volume scaled by the existing `battleLoud` (offвҶ’silent) AND the master capped low (вүӨ0.20, under the din's 0.26) so it never overwhelms the cues it sits under ("never jarring"). Located reports defer until the AudioContext is genuinely running (no first-gesture stampede); the bed self-silences on the 'over' screen (no idle-graph drain); source-voices node-pool bounded + all nodes disposed + context suspended on `fldExit`. CVD-safe (no colour-encoded info); the toggle row reuses T9's AA-vetted segmented-button markup (keyboard / focus / aria-pressed) вҶ’ `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern вҖ” 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity В· webaudio-leaks В· fog-leak В· edge-robust В· a11y-ux В· lifecycle] Г— 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 19 agents; critic confidence HIGH; "NO byte-identity violation, NO fog leak, marker-chain correct").** **1 confirmed + 2 critic-surfaced real edge-bugs + 1 LOW refinement, ALL FIXED:** **(CONFIRMED, MED, 3/3)** `fldAmbCaptionOnce` burned the one-shot `captioned` flag BEFORE the caption rendered вҖ” but T9's `_fldAudioCaption` no-ops when captions are off (the default), so a user enabling captions mid-battle would never see the cue the layer advertises вҶ’ the flag is now consumed ONLY inside the captions-on branch (re-checked cheaply each tick until shown). **(CRITIC, MED)** the six lenses only saw the probe's always-running context; in the real game the context is born SUSPENDED until a gesture, and located reports kept scheduling against the frozen clock вҶ’ a stacked "stampede" the instant audio resumed вҶ’ `fldAmbReports` now gates on `ctx.state === "running"`. **(CRITIC, LOW)** the live WebAudio graph idled indefinitely on the post-battle 'over' screen (master never zeroed there) вҶ’ `fldAmbUpdate` now silences on `phase === "over"`. **(CRITIC, LOW)** StereoPanner nodes shared the source bag, diluting the documented voice cap + a dead `.stop()` per dispose вҶ’ panners moved to a separate `pans` pool (cap counts audible voices only; panners disconnect-only). The lifecycle "stale per-phase state" finding was REFUTED 3/3 (singleton `__FIELD`; a negative men-delta clamps to 0; cooldowns expire across the interphase card вҖ” benign). Probe strengthened 19вҶ’22 steps (the suspended-ctx gate, the 'over'-silence, the panner-pool disposal).
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-audio-ambience` **22/22** (module + 4 wrappers В· opt-in activates + beds built + located reports scheduled В· pan вҲҲ [-1,1] В· separate panner pool В· suspended-ctx defers (0 reports/0 errors) В· 'over' self-silence В· sim-seed INVARIANT across 240 pure audio ticks В· `errN===0` В· accessible panel row В· DEFAULT-OFF silent В· reduceMotion suppressed В· `battleLoud="off"` master silent В· fog-gated 5вҶ’0 with lift-control 3 В· `fldExit` disposes beds+pools+ref В· 0 pe); `probe-presets` **26/26** (byte-identity вҶ’ combat byte-identical, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` **18/18** (T16 + marker chain) / `probe-weather` **30/30** (T17) / `probe-render-richness` **30/30** (T18) вҖ” all coexist; `probe-tactical-visuals` **10/10** (0 texture warnings); `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 14/14; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`. ## D129 вҖ” PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") В· H3-i3: **TERRAIN & UNIT RENDER RICHNESS** вҖ” procedural ground texture + woods wind-sway + banner cloth ripple + selection/march polish + casualty fade вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
The next Phase-H increment after H3-i2 (D128), per `.tmp/phase-h-design.md` item 3. A NEW presentation-only module makes the battlefield itself feel alive вҖ” the ground grows real texture, the woods sway, the colours ripple, marching columns bob, and a fallen brigade fades from the field instead of snapping out. Continues leading H with the code-only / single-file-safe / offline procedural wins before the external PD-imagery/footage layer (H1/H2, still to be SURFACED before starting).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js` вҖ” (1) **3D ground vertex-colour enrichment** (procedural grass mottle + dry-ochre / damp-lush / bare-earth patches + tilled crop-row corduroy in a "cultivated" mask вҖ” positions untouched, colours only); (2) **woods wind-sway** (per-cone tilt-about-base on the InstancedMesh); (3) **banner cloth ripple** (per-unit flag twist/dip, ties H1b flags); (4) **selection-ring pulse** + a **march bob** for moving brigades; (5) a **casualty fade-out** on death (the group settles into the ground + fades over ~0.85s). Plus 2D-canvas equivalents (a cached soft field-grain, a pulsing selection halo, the same casualty fade).
- **ARCHITECTURE вҖ” combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dBuildTerrain` (enrich + capture) / `fld3dRender` (frame hook) / `fld3dSyncUnit` (per-unit polish) / `fld2dDraw` (2D) / `fldExit` (dispose) BY ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16/T17 seam; propagates the `._wx`/`._atmo` markers so the wrapper chain stays introspectable). All variation is **analytic value-noise + wall-clock sines вҖ” NEVER `fldRng`**; reads ONLY render state + read-only sim fields (`u.x`/`u.z`/`u.alive`/`u.state`/`u.id`, `__FIELD.sel`); writes NO sim field, no `_SAVE_VER`. The ground enrichment recolors VERTICES only вҖ” units seat on the analytic `fldTerrainH`, not the mesh, so they never float/sink. **THE BYTE-IDENTICAL DEFAULT:** `renderRich="off"` (or a fresh launch with it set) leaves the un-enriched ground + unswayed woods + flat flags. Diff = `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T18 after T17) + `tools/probe-render-richness.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML. **No combat/data/save file touched** вҖ” proven by `probe-presets` 26/26 byte-identity AND a new per-burst sim-field-invariance probe assertion (x/z/men/morale/facing/formation unchanged across 200 render frames).
- **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** every MOTION effect (woods sway, flag ripple, selection pulse, march bob, casualty fade) is suppressed under `reduceMotion` вҖ” the STATIC ground texture stays (faithful detail, not motion; the T17 precedent). `renderRich="off"` disables the whole layer (motion reverts mid-battle; the 3D ground tint reverts on the next launch вҖ” the T16/T17 apply-time pattern, documented). The woods sway recomputes each instance matrix from a cached base (no drift); `fldLow()` trims sway amplitude + grain cell size; the **2D field-grain is cached to an offscreen canvas** (built once per field/scale, blitted with one `drawImage` вҖ” no per-frame fillrate on the weakest 2D-fallback GPU). No new draw call/shader вҶ’ no `gl_PointSize` concern. CVD-safe (texture carries no colour-encoded info); no new DOM/text вҶ’ `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.
- **Bug-hunt (the ultracode pattern вҖ” 6 diverse-lens Opus finders [byte-identity В· render-math В· perf В· a11y-gating В· edge-robust В· lifecycle] Г— 3-skeptic default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 37 agents; critic confidence HIGH).** **1 substantive bug + 7 real LOWs, ALL FIXED:** **(the one substantive defect, MED/HIGH across 4 lenses, 3/3 votes)** the casualty-fade `g.position.y -= (1-rec.fade)*5` was CUMULATIVE вҖ” the base `fld3dSyncUnit` early-returns for a dead unit and never re-seats its Y, so the per-frame decrement compounded to ~125 yards of sink (frame-rate dependent), plunging the fading brigade through the terrain instead of the intended ~5yd settle вҶ’ **rewritten ABSOLUTE** (`g.position.y = fldTerrainH(u.x,u.z)+4 - (1-f)*5`), bounded + frame-rate-independent (probe now asserts `maxSink вүӨ 8`; measured 4.96). Pure visual glitch вҖ” no sim write, D74 intact (the finders + critic confirmed). **(LOW, real)** the fade had no visibility guard вҶ’ a fog-hidden enemy that died popped into view as a fading block (a fog-of-war leak) вҶ’ guarded on `rec.wasVis` (the base's last-living-frame visibility) + a white-box probe test. **(critic-found LOWs)** a SELECTED unit that died kept its ring at full opacity over the fading ghost вҶ’ the ring now fades with the corpse; the fade-end `transparent=false` flip corrupted the textured T10 flag's alpha (latent) вҶ’ `_rrSetGroupOpacity` never flips the flag/ring transparent flag; the 2D grain was re-filled (~1300 `fillRect`s) every frame вҶ’ offscreen-canvas cache; `renderRich="off"` toggled mid-battle didn't revert the motion effects вҶ’ the early-return was removed so the motion-off reset paths run; the probe only proved seed-stability (not sim-field invariance) вҶ’ added the x/z/men/morale/facing snapshot; the empty-catch wrappers swallowed per-unit throws silently вҶ’ a counted + once-warned `FLDRR_S.errN` the probe asserts is 0. **Probe strengthened 24вҶ’30 steps.**
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK`; `probe-render-richness` **30/30** (module + 5 wrappers + chain markers В· ground enriched [meanAbsDelta 0.0178, 92% of vertices changed] + positions untouched В· woods sway/reset В· flag ripple/reset В· selection pulse В· casualty fade visible+opacity-in-(0,1)+BOUNDED-sink+fog-ghost-guarded+hidden-when-done В· sim seed + sim-field INVARIANT В· `errN===0` В· `renderRich="off"` un-enriched/unswayed/flat В· reduceMotion keeps texture suppresses motion В· 2D paints, 0 pe); `probe-presets` **26/26** (byte-identity вҶ’ combat byte-identical, re-confirmed post-fix); `probe-atmospherics` **18/18** (T16 coexists); `probe-weather` **30/30** (T17 coexists); `probe-tactical-visuals` **10/10** (all 9 battles render, 0 texture warnings); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; `bootprobe` realErrors:[]; `t1probe` 0 fails/0 pe. VISUALLY CONFIRMED (the field reads as real terrain with patches + tilled stripes; woods sway, flags ripple in the live battles). **NEXT in H3/H4:** H4 audio deepening вҶ’ H1b flags/insignia polish вҶ’ H1/H2 PD imagery + reenactment footage (**SURFACE first** вҖ” external assets / network / single-file stress). **Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles LAST** (Aaron's locked queue). (Reversible; non-negotiables honored вҖ” D74 no sim write + the empirical-vet-before-push gate.)

## D128 вҖ” PHASE H (graphics "make it come to life") В· H3-i2: **WEATHER + TIME-OF-DAY ATMOSPHERE** вҖ” procedural sky/light re-tint + rain/snow precipitation per a citation-grade per-battle weather hint вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-24)
The natural successor to H3-i1 (D127). A NEW presentation-only module gives each battle a sky and light that match its history. Designed + data-scoped at `.tmp/phase-h-design.md`. Continues leading Phase H with the code-only / single-file-safe / offline procedural wins before the external PD-imagery/footage layer (H1/H2, still to be SURFACED before starting).
- **What shipped:** new `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` вҖ” re-tints the 3D `scene.background` / `scene.fog` / sun (directional) / hemisphere AND washes the 2D canvas to a resolved `{sky, time}` palette (sky вҲҲ clear/overcast/rain/fog/haze/snow; time вҲҲ dawn/morning/midday/afternoon/dusk), plus optional procedural **rain/snow precipitation** (a second `THREE.Points` cloud reusing the T16 shader pattern) and a faint 2D precip hatch. A one-time accessible **weather note** is announced at battle start via the existing role=status `fldScenarioBanner`. **Marquee visible win: Antietam's dawn Cornfield ground-fog** (the one genuinely non-clear sky in the roster); the rest carry faithful time-of-day light (warm afternoons, cool mornings).
- **ARCHITECTURE вҖ” combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dInit` (re-tint) / `fld3dRender` (precip + note) / `fld2dDraw` (wash + note) / `fldExit` (dispose) BY ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16 seam; propagates T16's `._atmo` marker so the wrapper chain stays introspectable). ## D121 вҖ” E2 increment 2: **THE INLINE GLOSSARY** вҖ” hover/tap/focus codex definitions woven into the teaching prose вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped:** the second E2 / S4-education item вҖ” an INLINE GLOSSARY. New `src/93-glossary.js` DOM-decorates the rendered teaching prose of the two read-only teaching desk tabs (After-Action, Your War vs History): a TreeWalker wraps codex terms in inline `<button class="gl-term">` triggers (a dotted brass underline) and a shared `#glTip` tooltip shows the definition on hover/focus/tap. It reads the SAME codex data as the i1 Codex tab (`cxGlossaryIndex`/`cxLookupShort`) вҖ” one source of truth. Hooked into `_wdRefresh` (guarded, scoped to afteraction/warvshistory), byte-identical when absent.
- **ACCESSIBILITY-FIRST:** the definition rides each trigger's `aria-label` ("<visible matched text> вҖ” <short> (glossary term)") so a screen-reader announces it on FOCUS regardless of the visual tooltip; the tooltip is `aria-hidden` role=tooltip decorative reinforcement (no double-announce). Triggers are real keyboard-operable `<button>`s; Esc dismisses; a scoped `:focus-visible` ring; reduce-motion disables the tooltip transition; the cue is a dotted UNDERLINE (shape), not color-alone. wcag-auditor AA (tooltip 13.51:1, term/border 8.10:1; no edits).
- **Surface-derivation (the keystone design):** matchers are built from DERIVED SURFACES, not the raw `en.term` вҖ” the core noun phrase (leading "The " + trailing "(...)" clarifier stripped), any parenthetical acronym (e.g. "(USCT)" вҶ’ USCT), and authored aliases вҖ” so the spellings prose ACTUALLY uses match (e.g. "The Lost Cause (Myth)" вҶ’ "Lost Cause"; "United States Colored Troops (USCT)" вҶ’ "United States Colored Troops" + "USCT"). High-value bare-form **aliases** added to 3 codex entries (emancipation, blockade/Anaconda Plan, conscription/draft) вҖ” pure data the codex already supports.
- **Architecture вҖ” PURE READ-OUT (byte-identical combat BY CONSTRUCTION):** `glDecorate` reads `GAME_DATA.codex` (via cx accessors) and DECORATES already-rendered DOM; it WRITES NOTHING to the sim (no campaign state, no save, no RNG). No tactical/combat/tick/resolve/bridge path references `gl*` (grep-confirmed + a probe static-scan over 20 combat files) вҶ’ battles byte-identical by construction. The `_wdRefresh` hook clears `data-gl-done` before each render (the reused `#wdContent` element) so re-viewing a teaching tab re-decorates. Diff = `src/93-glossary.js` + `data/codex.json` (3 aliases) + `src/00-manifest.json` (`93-glossary.js`) + `src/30-president-shell.js` (the guarded hook) + `tools/probe-glossary.mjs` + the generated HTML.

## D113 вҖ” В§12.3 THE ELECTION-SUPPORT RELIEF-BIND вҖ” a commissioned political general costs more capital to relieve before the 1864 vote (the bind Lincoln lived) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped (the GM В§12.3 keystone the Commission move D109 was built around, now unblocked by the 1864-election state E4/D112):** a commissioned POLITICAL general (Banks/Butler/Sigel/McClernand вҖ” `commission.kind:"political"` + a `politicalValue`) delivers his constituency's votes to the war effort while he serves, so relieving him in the run-up to the 1864 election forfeits that support вҖ” an ADDITIVE surcharge on his relief cost (`_cmdReliefCost`) that rises year over year toward the vote (1862<1863<1864) and FALLS to zero the moment `clock.resolved1864` is set (the bind is spent). `surcharge = round((politicalValue/100) * windowByYear[year] * surchargeMax)`, bounded [0, surchargeMax=14]. A new teaching tell on the active-general card names the constituency + the `+N capital` cost ("Lincoln lived this bind"). Teaches the В§12.3 command-politics lesson concretely: Banks in command costs commandLeadership 49 vs Grant's 87 (D109) AND can't be cheaply dumped before November 1864.

## D110 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER** (seat pool generals into division billets nested under a seated corps вҖ” the next rung of the GM depth-chart over the OOB tree) вҖ” [CODEX code + CLAUDE close-out] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The next rung of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.1's billet tree (Army вҶ’ Corps вҶ’ **DIVISION** вҶ’ Brigade), built HIERARCHICALLY on the Q10 corps depth-chart (D108). Beyond seating the army's IвҖ“IV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **DIVISION** billets (3 per corps), spending `seatCost` (2) political capital (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the existing GM currency, no new resource per В§12). A division is staffable ONLY UNDER a SEATED corps (the real chain of command вҖ” a division belonged to a corps), so the depth chart becomes a TREE the President builds top-down.
- **PROVENANCE / CLOSE-OUT (the [AARON] hand-off):** the Q12 CODE + DATA + PROBE were authored in an interrupted Claude-Code session, finished + committed (`7b64d2e`) + pushed by **Codex** on this machine. Codex shipped a sound, builds-GATE-OK, byte-identical-to-source feature **but did NOT run the adversarial bug-hunt or write any doc trail** (a PROPER-VETTING gap vs CLAUDE.md #3 + a record-in-repo gap vs #5). This entry + the bug-hunt below are the **CLAUDE close-out** that brings D110 to the project's "done" bar. (No code was reverted вҖ” the commit is sound; this adds the missing vetting + documentation, plus the one bug-hunt fix.)
- **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only shape the army's LEADERSHIP facet вҖ” an INPUT the bridge already reads вҖ” via a small BOUNDED lift folded into `commandLeadership`, summed exactly like the corps lift: `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(ОЈ over seated divisions of (`effDivRating`вҲ’64)Г—`perSlotWeight`, Вұ`liftCap`) = clamp(ОЈГ—0.03, Вұ2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (`_cmdGenRating`, carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his current grade is below `preferredGrade`. The lift is DELIBERATELY SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4, weight 0.03 vs 0.05) so the influence hierarchy holds вҖ” **army (~Вұ17, В§27) > corps (Вұ4) > divisions (Вұ2):** a lower tier is a smaller modifier, never dominant. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership вҶ’ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG.
- **THE GRADE-FIT (a division was a Maj. Gen.'s billet in BOTH armies):** `preferredGrade` is a bare Maj. Gen. for US and CS alike вҖ” distinct from the corps tier (a US corps a Maj. Gen.'s, a CS corps a Lt. Gen.'s). Many divisions were in fact led by Brigadier Generals early in the war, so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads `belowGrade` until promoted (the Q9 synergy, biting on both sides here). `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand`: perCorps 3 В· seatCost 2 В· preferredGrade {US,CS: "Maj. Gen."} В· perSlotWeight 0.03 В· liftCap 2 В· belowGradePenalty 4 В· **Inferred** В· 2 real sources (Glatthaar, *General Lee's Army*; Weigley, *A Great Civil War*).
- **BYTE-IDENTICAL until you seat a division:** no division seated вҶ’ the ОЈ is over zero slots вҶ’ lift 0 вҶ’ `commandLeadership` unchanged вҶ’ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf` (a vacant division contributes 0, NOT a penalty; `_cmdDivLift` has a fast-path returning 0 without walking the roster when `cmd.divisions` is empty/absent вҖ” so a pre-Q12 save with no record reads identically). **ONE BILLET PER MAN:** a general holds at most one of {army command, a corps, a division}; seating him in a division clears any corps/other division he held, and appointing/seating him HIGHER clears his division. **Vacating a corps CASCADES** вҖ” its orphaned divisions stop contributing lift, enforced at the READ layer (`cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift` filter divisions whose parent corps is no longer seated; `_cmdDivClean`:795 requires the parent corps seated) and cleaned on the next load-sanitize. `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:generalId}}` (nested) rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop array/non-object/out-of-range/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/dupes вҖ” the Q9/Q10/Q11 idiom). Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + `C.clock.capital`. Carries the Q9/Q10/Q11 hardening verbatim: the `isFinite` capital guard, the commission gate (`_cmdByIdRoster`+`cmdCommissioned`), and debit-the-rounded-gate-value.
- **THE TEACHING (anti-Lost-Cause, both sides):** a corps was only as good as its divisions вҖ” A. P. Hill's hard-hitting "Light Division" and Hood's and Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions under Hancock's II Corps (Gibbon, Barlow)** вҖ” while a corps with weak divisions underdelivered. New UI: division sub-rows nested under each seated corps in the "The Corps Command вҖ” Depth Chart" section + a combined corps+division lift read-out; every new colour annotated вүҘ4.5:1 (WCAG-AA), every dynamic value `_cmdEsc`-escaped.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (the close-out Codex skipped вҖ” run NOW on the shipped diff):** a Workflow of **5 diverse-lens Opus finders** (no-fudge/byte-identity В· economy/determinism/bounding В· citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers В· XSS/escaping В· UI/edge/save-tamper) Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic. **4 lenses CLEAN; 1 confirmed LOW, FIXED:** the division teaching exemplars (A. P. Hill's Light Division, Hood's, Pickett's) were **all-Confederate** while the rating mechanism is genuinely side-neutral and the sibling corps tier deliberately named both sides (the rout of Howard's XI Corps) вҖ” the exact Lost-Cause over-celebration pattern CLAUDE.md #4 guards against. FIXED (copy-only, byte-identical): added the Union counterpart (Hancock's II Corps divisions, Gibbon/Barlow вҖ” accurate at Gettysburg/Wilderness/Spotsylvania) to both the player-facing `divFoot` string and the `divisionCommand` `_note`. The save-tamper lens independently executed an 18-vector battery against `_cmdDivClean` (Array/null/non-object/out-of-range/float-key/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/cross-corps-dupe) вҖ” all sanitize correctly; the no-fudge lens grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.divisions`; escaping confirmed safe (`htmlEsc` at render + `_cmdEsc` in the UI).
- **Vetting (the offline gates GREEN; the headless `load` suite ENV-BLOCKED):** `GATE OK В· no-fudge вң“ В· citations вң“`; the committed `civil_war_generals.html` is **byte-identical to the source build** (empty post-build diff); `probe-command` **69/69** (+11 Q12 steps: config + hierarchy [div liftCap < corps liftCap], byte-identical-when-empty + absent-record, the hierarchy gate [division only under a seated corps], spend/gate/re-seat/vacate, the read-layer cascade, one-billet-per-man, render) with **0 pageerrors**; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346` (Classic paints); `t1probe` + `bootprobe` ok. **No tactical/combat file is in the D110 diff** (`src/35-command.js` + `data/ratings.json` + `tools/probe-command.mjs` + the generated HTML only) вҶ’ the 9 battles are byte-identical to Q11 **by construction**. **ENV:** the strategic no-regression `load` battery (`probe-desk/ratings/camp/officers/field/oob` + the 9 battle probes) was blocked by the documented **THREE-CDN headless `load`-stall** вҖ” jsdelivr rate-limited this machine's headless client after the first clean load, so only the first chromium launch per session loads (re-running the known-good `probe-command` reproduced the stall on demand); these probes share NO Q12 code path and were all GREEN in the Q11 vetting hours earlier. ## D109 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q11: THE COMMISSION MOVE** (bring documented POLITICAL GENERALS into the officer pool for political capital; the GM "Commission" move) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The GM depth-chart move of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.2/В§12.3 ("Commission вҖ” bring a new officer into the pool"). Beyond the generals the war hands you, the President may now **COMMISSION the documented POLITICAL GENERALS** вҖ” US **Banks**, **Butler**, **Sigel**, **McClernand**; CS **Floyd**, **Pillow** вҖ” into his officer pool for **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the existing GM currency, no new resource per В§12), after which they are appointable / promotable / seatable like any general. A new Command-desk **"Commission an officer вҖ” the political generals"** section lists each with his (LOW) combat OVR beside his (HIGH) political value, his constituency, an honest one-line record, and a Commission control (gated on capital + the `maxCommissions` slate). Teaches the GM layer's central command-politics lesson (В§12.3, the keystone): political generals were **cheap to commission and weak in the field** вҖ” Lincoln and Davis took them for the factions, votes, and immigrant regiments they delivered, not their generalship вҖ” so once you appoint or seat one, his low OVR drags the army's leadership, the bind Lincoln lived. **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose Commission (option C) over the symmetric AI-GM (B, [hard]) and the DIVISION sub-tier (B-alt, lower-risk-but-thinner) because it fills the GM layer's missing teaching keystone (the political-general bind the В§12.3 anti-gamey constraints are built around), uses the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdPromote` byte-identical-until-used spine + the В§8 person concept, and adds 6 new citation-grade historical figures. Scoped to a **pure pool-addition move** (no economy/election fork); the full В§12.3 election-support relief-bind is logged as the explicit next increment (it needs the 1864-election state вҖ” here the relief COST is already taught via each officer's `relief` class through `_cmdReliefCost`).
- **ARCHITECTURE (byte-identical until the player commissions):** the commissionable officers live in a SEPARATE data array (`data/generals.json` вҶ’ `sides[side].commissionPool`), so `_cmdSideGenerals` (the starting roster) and every byte-identity-critical path are UNTOUCHED. `cmdCommission` writes ONLY `cmd.commissioned` (an id list) + `C.clock.capital` + a reputation seed вҖ” NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). With nobody commissioned, `_cmdRosterPlusCommissioned` === the bare roster (`roster.concat([])`), so the appoint/promote/corps pools, `commandLeadership`, and the 9 battles are identical to HEAD `8eb913a`. A commissioned officer reaches the fight ONLY by being appointed/seated like any general вҖ” no new combat read. `_cmdById` was widened to also resolve the commission pool (so a commissioned-then-appointed officer resolves everywhere); `_cmdByIdRoster` keeps the roster-only lookup for the byte-identity-critical seeds + the commission "not-a-roster-id" guard. `cmd.commissioned` rides the save; `cmdInit` seeds `[]` once + SANITIZES on load (drop dupes / bogus ids / roster ids / over-cap; non-array вҶ’ array вҖ” the Q9/Q8b/Q10 idiom). NO `_SAVE_VER` bump. NO RNG.
- **THE TEACHING (rank вү  competence; anti-Lost-Cause, both sides):** the 6 are authored with LOW combat OVR / HIGH political value вҖ” appointing a commissioned Banks fields commandLeadership **49** vs Grant's **87** (probe-verified). Honest records name the failures plainly on BOTH sides (Banks/Red River, Butler/Fort Fisher, Sigel/New Market, McClernand/Vicksburg insubordination; Floyd & Pillow/the Fort Donelson flight) AND credit the genuine contributions (Butler's 1861 "contraband" decision; Banks's Louisiana free-labor/emancipation work). The combat ratings are stamped **Inferred** (a calibrated reading); the biographies carry вүҘ2 real published sources each (gate-4e-clean). Persona command/tactical/discipline are calibrated so `fldOfficerSkillSeed` rounds EXACTLY to the entry skill (the existing oracle; verified for all 6). Data authored via a 12-agent **research+verify Workflow** (6 Opus historians + adversarial source-check + a completeness critic); the verifier's one HARD correction applied вҖ” **Pillow's rank вҶ’ Brig. Gen.** (his "Maj. Gen." was a Mexican-War US-volunteer / Tennessee-state-militia title; in CSA service he rose only to brigadier вҖ” CLAUDE.md non-negotiable #4); plus Banks's Black-officer purge folded into his bio and Sigel's unconfirmed reprint year dropped.
- **DATA:** `data/generals.json` `sides.US.commissionPool` (us-banks/us-butler/us-sigel/us-mcclernand) + `sides.CS.commissionPool` (cs-floyd/cs-pillow); `data/ratings.json` `commission` config (costPolitical 2 В· costProfessional 8 В· maxCommissions 3 В· Inferred В· 2 src) + 6 new `generalPersonas`. - **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/byte-identity В· economy/determinism/bounding/cap В· citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers В· XSS/escaping В· UI/WCAG/edge] Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; **12 agents; invariantsHold = TRUE** вҖ” the critic independently grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.commissioned`, `cmdCommission` writes EXACTLY `cmd.commissioned`+capital+reputation, the byte-identity-when-empty property, Pillow correctly Brig.
